IRM: IRM-39395 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: TAXPAYER ACCOUNTING | Epic: Taxpayer Accounting Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Enable financial events logging under Org units and Claimants | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 1600 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Enable financial events logging under Org units and Claimants | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a revenue officer I need to be able to log financial transactions under Organization units related party roles and Claimants related party roles, as to be able to log into the system transactions that are related to offset vouchers , Revenue officer departments transfer orders (that are logged as org units) , Performing settlements and transfers with third parties (that are logged as claimants).

IRM: IRM-38899 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: TAX ACCOUNTS | Epic: Tax Accounts Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Support Tax Account Overview Page in the Single Taxpayer Overview | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GTM | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 350 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Support Tax Account Overview Page in the Single Taxpayer Overview | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a revenue officer, I want to have an overview of the financial transactions for a revenue type registration that represents a tax account, so that I can see an aggregated, holistic and coherent representation of the financial data of the the tax account in a specificied reconciliation period. 

*Introduction*

This feature describes the functional business requirements for a new single taxpayer overview page within Solon Tax, named the "Tax Account Overview". This new feature will introduce a period-centric overview. It will aggregate and present all financial transactions (FTs) related to a selected _reconciliation period(s)_ for a given revenue type registration, providing an immediate, consolidated view of that period's financial status. 

The purpose of this page is to provide a consolidated view of all Financial Transactions (FTs) associated with a specific reconciliation period for a taxpayer's Tax Account.

Currently, while Solon Tax supports the concept of a Tax Account ({{{}Skattekonto{}}}) and links Financial Transactions to reconciliation periods, there is no dedicated user interface that presents this information in a single, easily accessible view. This feature will bridge that gap, improving visibility and efficiency for Revenue Authority users managing these accounts.

As a reference countries that "Tax Account" is most prevalent in Europe, particularly in Scandinavia and the Nordics, which are global leaders in e-government. 

Currently implementation exists for the "Single Taxpayer Overview" pages, often refered to as 360 View, where a "Taxpayer Financial Overview" exists and can be used as reference. Particularly the last accordion of this page referred as " Financial Details per Financial Transaction". This is a page where all financial transactions for all revenue types are displayed and not only Tax Account that is the scope of this feature. 

*Functional Requirements*
h4. Navigation

A new redirect link shall be introduced on the *Revenue Type Registration (RTR)* page.
 * This link shall only be visible for RTRs that are configured as a "Tax Account" (i.e., where the {{isTaxAccount}} flag on the associated Revenue Type is true).
 * The link will navigate the user to the new "Tax Account Overview" page, passing the context of the current RTR and the selected reconciliation period.
 * Assumption is that the existing link from the party role will continue to function as is with the additional view in scope of this feature for the Tax Account. 

h4. Page Content and Layout

The "Tax Account Overview" page will contain the following elements:
 * *Filters:* User should be able to filter the following information:

 * 
 ** Reconciliation Period Filter
 ** From: 01/01/2026 
 ** To: 31/01/2026 or To: 31/03/2026, meaning more than one reconciliation periods can be selected. 

 
 * *"Update P&I" Button:* User should be able to see and select the "Update P&I" button where he/she can enter the "RECALCULATEFROMDATE" to run Penalty & Interest. 

 * *Financial Transactions Table:* A table displaying all Financial Transactions linked to the selected reconciliation period for the given Tax Account. The table should be read-only and provide standard functionalities like sorting, pagination and Column Configurator. The table should start with an opening balance for the period selected and end with the closing balance. 

Opening Balance of a period should be equal to the closing balance of the previous period. Opening balance should be the running balance of all financial transactions prior to date from selected in the filters. 

Closing Balance of a period is the running balance and should be equal to the Opening of that period plus any financial transaction related to that period such as debts, payments (both allocated and unallocated), interests, write offs, refunds... 

Available Columns (data) for FTs should be:  
 * Creation Date
 * Effective Date (eg. Period Reference - Period the debt/payment refers to)
 * Accounting Date 
 * Origin 
 * FT ID
 * Revenue Type 
 * FT Type 
 * Posting Reason
 * Liability Balance 
 * Running Balance

Please refer to the attached example_updated for a comprehensive view of the Tax Account Overview page.
h3. Assumptions & Dependencies
 * The Revenue Type entity has a configurable attribute to designate it as a "Tax Account."
 * The Financial Transaction entity has an attribute ({{{}reconciliationPeriodCode{}}}) to link it to a specific Reconciliation Period.

*Key features highlighted in this view:*
 * *Opening Balance:* The view starts with the "Opening Balance" showing the tax account's debt from before the selected period.
 * *Running Balance:* A column shows the balance after every single transaction, which is crucial for analysis.
 * *Detailed Descriptions:* Transactions are clearly labeled (e.g., "Payroll Tax Assessment," "Payment Received").
 * *Period Reference:* A column links a transaction back to the original tax period it relates to (e.g., Q4-2025), which is vital for an officer's investigation.

 

*Non functional requirements*
It is expected team to get aligned with respective teams and reassure that is not creating issues or the related NFRs will be tested :
Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability 
DODs should be fulfilled.

More over related to performance the team is expected to provide a solution on how the opening balance will be retrieved considering all past debts. Note that past debts may be related to periods, that may differ per revenue authority, for the last 10 years for example.  | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: This will provide Revenue Authority users with a clear, consolidated view of all financial activities within a specific reconciliation period for a taxpayer's Tax Account, improving efficiency and accuracy. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: * When I am on a revenue type registration for a Tax Account, I can see and click a "View Tax Account Overview" link for that RTR, more details specified in the functional requirements.
 * After clicking the link, I am navigated to a new page titled "Tax Account Overview" for that Tax Account.
 * As a User I am able to filter the from and to reconciliation periods I am interested to see financial transactions for, more details specified in the functional requirements. 
 * User should be able to see in the UI a Table with financial transactions is updated with an opening and closing balance as per attached example_updated and functional requirements in this feature, more details specified in the functional requirements.
 * User should be able to see and select the "Update P&I" button where he/she can enter the "RECALCULATEFROMDATE" to run Penalty & Interest. 
IRM: IRM-37845 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: REGISTRATION | Epic: Registration Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Enhance Validity period conditions in Registry detail entities to support multiple modifications in the same date | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 800 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Enhance Validity period conditions in Registry detail entities to support multiple modifications in the same date | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a revenue officer I need to be able to complete several Party details changes in the same date and system will allow this without effecting uniqueness and overlapping checks that are applied to Party and Party Role child entities with valid-from/valid-to periods.

The same logic must also apply when system determines which registry records are considered valid for a specific date (e.g., Today view in the UI or a historical date view).

The solution should be able to support same day changes for : 

a) records with valid-from/valid-to dates are considered duplicated or overlapping.
b) primary records with valid-from/valid-to dates are considered duplicated.
c) The criteria used to determine which records are valid on a specific reference date (current date or historical date).

*Functional requirements*

 

*New Fields* 
 * For all the above mentioned Party child objects, Party , Party Role, add Optional fields 
Valid State? , Boolean 
State Reason, Free text 
 * Make fields searchable
 * Make fields visible in the UI
 * Make fields updatable as/where the Valid from /to fields are
 * Move the information to relevant Party role sections (as Valid from/to) 
 * Default value of valid_state = true (e.g. when creating a record)
 ** All existing records are migrated with valid_state = true
 * (!)   Define if a record type should be checked for uniqueness or not 
Field: Check if unique?  /Boolean

*Rules for Unique record check:*

For the same record type (or per case additional filters are used, such as in Identifiers the country) 
If the record is flagged as Valid
check  if the period is not overlapping other periods 
In case of end date = other records start date then the end date overlapping with other record start date is ignored. (i.e. only end date of one period is the same as the start date of another period, see bullet 4) 
 # If a record  flag Valid? = false : it is ignored during uniqueness checks and for primary checks.
 # If a record  flag CheckifUnique? = false : it is ignored during uniqueness checks and for primary checks.   (!)
 # If a record Start date = End date= Y  , Flag Valid ? = true  : record is selected primary or considered proper entry for date Y   (primary set for start date Y,  if flagged as primary) 
 # If  Record 1 start date end = A  and end date = X  , valid = true
and Record 2 start date = X , end date = B , valid = true
both  flag Valid? = true ,  
Then these records are not considered overlapping (although in current rule are consider overlapping). 
On date X, the valid record is Record2 (the record with start date X)
Not the one with end date = X (Record 1).
 # If Record1: start date is null , end date  = X  , valid = true
Record2: start date  = X , end date  = null  , valid = true
The record 2 is selected primary or the considered for date x 
 # If Record1: start date is null , end date  = null  , valid = true
Record2: start date  = X , end date  = null   , valid = true
 System will not allow this because of overlapping in other days (!)
 # If two records of the same type, 
and both have Valid state = true, 
when their validity periods overlap (e.g. 5) , the system rejects the change due to overlapping validity periods. (!)
 # A record is considered for date D when: 
valid state = true and 
start date <= D  and End date is null or end date > D , valid = true
 # If multiple changes occur in the same transaction, Uniqueness validation must run after final state.
 # Notes:
 ## If valid to = null means infinite validity
 ## API queries using reference dates follow the same validity rules
 ## the  included fields in uniqueness checks already considered (e.g. in Identities the countries, or the type of the record) should continue be used.

 

*Apply to :*
 * Validation of Uniqueness of primary records per period
 * Validation of Uniqueness of records per type (and other flags as per entity) per period
 * Define the visibly records that defines the view of today, history date, date in the past 

*UI :*

 Filter history records by valid from 
 If valid_state = false , state_reason must be populated

IRM: IRM-37844 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: TAXPAYER ACCOUNTING | Epic: Taxpayer Accounting Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: GL decisions table - Multiline rules and additional parameters /Functionality & Reference Implementation | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 1600 | Priority: p2 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: GL decisions table - Multiline rules and additional parameters /Functionality & Reference Implementation | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As an administrator responsible for defining the Accountant table details, I need to introduce additional parameters that determine how GL accounts are selected based on the accounting rules of FT types. Specifically, I need to support differentiating GL accounting rules according to the claimant, revenue type, and bill segment type categorization. 

These new parameters will enable the system to efficiently handle the many hundreds of special cases that must be supported, reduce the size of the GL decision table and the number of FT types, and overall improve the systems maintainability and administration.

 

*Functional Requirements* 

 

*Valid From/To columns*
 * Add columns Valid from / Valid to (as Datetime ) in GL Decision Table(s)
 * if empty valid from to is empty , consider line as valid.
 * Rules should consider the validity based on these fields.
 * Advise in documentation and code the format of the field. 

 

*Multilines* 

In several situations one FT may be detailed in several gl accounts i.e., several journal entries lines. 
Similarly to what is implemented in Assessments calculation lines, because of different cost centers , several gl accounts should be changed in one transaction based on a rule on how to split these amounts.  
 * In GL decision spreadsheets, Define of an Accounting rule included many lines to finally define the journal entries needed. 
 * Add an indication per line like line 1,2,3
 * Define the rule on how to split the amount (e.g. per percentage to original FT amount. the total amount should be same as FT amount or an error will block the journal entries creation because of FT validation rules ) .

!image-2026-03-02-23-45-16-740.png|width=688,height=278!

*Rules logic*
 * If the parameter/condition is empty, it should be ignored by the rules. 
 * Rules should search for all the lines that the conditions are fulfilled and check the valid from to.
 * GL Account Code for Gain/loss may be null and should be ignored in primary currency mode. 

 

*Customers may add new parameters as columns in gl decision tabels and use in drools*
 * Customers should know based on documented instructions,  how to add their own parameters in the Gl_decision drools sheets and use them in relevant drools rules.
 *  *Reference implementation* /example columns
 ** Revenue Type,
 ** Accounting Date
 ** Claimant? (Yes /No)  ,  Claimant type/ID    
 ** Segment Type (Bill segment, Payment, Allocation) , Segment Category     Segment Subcategory    
 ** (as -is) FT Type Category  , Financial Transaction Accounting Date 
 ** Action (Create . Cancel)
 ** Add a no functional logic "Notes" column
 * Customers should be able to add their own parameters and get the parameters from FT record.
 ** Columns for  Custom Parameter A (e.g. Reference year), Custom Parameter B  (e.g. DOY) , Custom Parameter C    (these may be ignored if customers can add their columns if/when needed.  
 ** Considerations : Customers may need to add conditions/Parameters on FT details, or Party details, or RTR details and these details may be also captured in data areas.  

 

*Correction future proof for multicurrency*
Replace the one column GL Account Code for Gain/loss with 2 
GL Account Code for Gain/loss/ CREDIT (MAKE IT NULLABLE)    
GL Account Code for Gain/loss/ DEBIT (MAKE IT NULLABLE) , leave it null in reference implementation sheet.

IRM: IRM-37825 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: BILLING, ASSESSMENTS AND INSTALLMENTS | Epic: Billing & Assessments Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Transfer Amount - Enhancement on configuration of Bill segment types | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 320 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Transfer Amount - Enhancement on configuration of Bill segment types | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As an admin, I need to configure the bill segment types generated by the Transfer Amount process so they align with existing, predefined bill segment configurations used in other relevant procedures (e.g., for the same revenue types and bill segment categories).

In the as-is, one Bill segment type is defined and be used for source and target bill segments.

 

*Functional Requirements*

 

*A) New Bill Segment Type field, next to existing:* 
 * Alternative Target Bill segment type 
Lookup bill segment type and filters may be used to locate proper type.
 * Optional field
 * Add Tooltip: This value applies to the target bill segment if filled. If no filled the default bill segment type will be applied to target bill segment as in source bill segment. 
 * Add it in search filters.

*B) Existing Bill Segment Type field:*
 * New label : Default Bill segment type
 * Be able to search by  using fields to locate proper type.
 * Add Tooltip: This value applies to the source bill segment and will also be applied to the target bill segment unless a different bill segment type is explicitly selected.

Consideration : Bill type should support both bill segment types. 

 

*C) Mechanism:*
 * Default bill segment type is mandatory. 
 * Default Bill segment type will be used for source bill segment.
 * Alternative Target Bill segment type  will be used for target bill segment.
 * If Alternative Target Bill segment type id not filled, then Default Bill segment type will be used for target bill segment.

 

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments. 

*Non functional requirements*

Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability

IRM: IRM-30362 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: TAXPAYER ACCOUNTING | Epic: Taxpayer Accounting Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: GL decisions table - Ensure extensibility and high volume support of decisions /Functionality & Reference Implementation | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 1600 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: GL decisions table - Ensure extensibility and high volume support of decisions /Functionality & Reference Implementation | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As an administrator responsible for configuring the GL Decision Table (Accountant table), iI need to support the extensibility of the solution. 
I need to introduce additional parameters that control how GL accounts are split across multiple files or tables. This is required to support very high volumes of decision lines and complex business rules.
I need to allow custom adapters to be used on how rules are created and selected to generate journal entries. 

These parameters will allow the system to efficiently handle hundreds of special cases, reduce the size and complexity of individual GL decision tables, and improve maintainability by splitting configurations into multiple, logically grouped records. 

A realistic number of GL decision lines with the assumption that legacy GLs will be removed from time to time, is 200.000 lines

 

*Functional Requirements* 


+*1.* Some suggestions on how to support high volumes of rules:+ 

*A) GL Decision Line Volume Support*
 * Decision rule sheets must support modern XLSX row limits (1,048,576+ rows), not legacy XLS limits (65,536 rows).
 * The system should support the use of multiple decision lines per transaction (multi-lines), where applicable.

*B) Split GL Decision Tables Across Multiple Sheets or Files*
 * As an admin/configurator, I must be able to define and use more than one spreadsheet or files for GL Decision Tables.
 * Splitting must be rule-driven and configurable.

*C) Rule Evaluation Mechanism*

The system must determine which spreadsheet(s) to read based on configured split rules.
One FT may require reading:

A single sheet, or Multiple sheets, depending on customer-defined configuration.
Rule evaluation must be deterministic and transparent (traceable which sheets were evaluated).

 

*D)   Reference Implementation Split Strategies (Examples)*
 * The system should support splitting GL decision tables based on configurable parameters, such as FT Origin, RTR relation with Claimants etc: 
 ** Segment type of Origin  of Financial transactions (ft_origin_cl) , splitting spreadsheets for Bill segments, Payment segments, Allocation Segments. 
One sheet for Segment type = Bill segment, one for Payment Segments, one Allocation Segments
 ** If Claimant related (if the revenue type registration is related to a claimant) 
Use a dedicated spreadsheet containing claimant-specific GL mappings.
i.e., If a revenue type is related to a specific claimant, the system reads only the claimant-specific sheet.
 ** The revenue type, Domain
Certification-related mappings in one sheet. 
All other revenue/tax types in separate sheets.
Additional Parameters as reference implementation in GL Decision Table [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-37721] 
 ** Considerations : Customers may also add a rule, to read for every FT,  2 or more sheets,  as the rules sheet may split per Ledger.   (The system reads from two or more sheets per FT, e.g. one per Ledger.) 
Other cases may include parameters to split on segment type category/subcategory or revenue type details and some of these details may be also captured in data areas.


+2. Expandability+

*E) Customers are able to use custom in process implementation*
Be able to adjust a custom implementation in process to run in order  to create journal entries. Interface (as in allocation) to feed the results in Solon Journal entries

 

*Documentation*

All configuration options, split strategies, and rule evaluation logic must be fully documented.

Documentation must include:
 * Usage and Configuration examples
 * Reference implementations
 * Operational guidelines , Performance considerations

*Non functional requirements*

*Security*  no exposure of sensitive configuration data
*Accessibility*  configuration screens and documentation must remain accessible
*Usability*  splitting logic must be understandable and maintainable by admins

IRM: IRM-29430 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: PENALTY & INTEREST | Epic: Penalty & Interest Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Enhance Credit Interest Calculation to include unallocated payment segments | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GTM | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 3200 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Enhance Credit Interest Calculation to include unallocated payment segments | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a revenue authority officer I would like Solon RM to consider in credit interest calculation, all payments received from a taxpayer, both allocated and unallocated, so that final interest calculation is accurate and can be used in relevant processes.  

*Introduction*
This feature was originally introduced for SKV implementation of Reimbursement Interest in [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-15910] the credits from Bill segments are considered in the calculations. To complete this interest calculation, system needs to consider all payment segments as well. 

Moving forward for the implemetation of the Tax Account in Northern countries but also for other implementations, in order to calculate interest accurately all payment segments, allocated and unallocated needs to be considered.  

Update the existing CREDIT_INT PI (Penalty & Interest) rule to calculate reimbursement interest on credit unallocated payment segments for tax account scenarios, ensures taxpayers receive proper interest on all credit amounts.

Currently, the system calculates interest only on bill segment balances. However, when for example liability amendments occur (e.g., reducing a VAT liability from 100 to 80 after a 100 payment has been made), the resulting 20 credit unallocated payment segment does not accrue interest in favor of the taxpayer. This creates an unfair situation where taxpayer funds held by the tax authority do not earn the required interest. 

To enhance understanding of this feature and facilitate analysis tasks please find below a business example as well as business cases where Solon Tax results in unallocated payment segments.

*System Requirements*
 * PI Rule Enhancement: Rule Code = CREDIT_INT (Reimbursement Interest Rule) Enhancement: Update calculation logic to include credit unallocated payment segments (next to credits on bill segments that is already implemented). 

*Business Example*

> Initial State:

VAT Liability: 100 (debit)

Payment Made: 100 (credit)

Result: Liability fully paid, balance = 0

> After Amendment:

Amendment: VAT liability reduced by 20 (becomes 80)

Payment Remains: 100 (unchanged)

Result: 20 credit unallocated payment segment

_Current Behavior:_

Interest calculated only on bill segment balances, thus 20 credit unallocated payment segment earns no interest

_Required Behavior:_

Interest calculated on bill segment balances AND credit unallocated payment segments, thus 20 credit unallocated payment segment earns monthly interest in favor of taxpayer

 

*Example Business Cases resulting in Unallocated Payment Segments*
 # Payment Suspense Scenarios, where for example invalid reference number results to a payment that cannot be allocated to a specific party role.
 # Payment File Processing Errors during automated payment file processing due to for example corrupted payment data or reference number mismatch.
 # Insufficient liability balance for full allocation as per the business example above. 
 # Payment Event State Transitions, when for example re-opening completed payment events where original segments need to be cancelled or payment event re-distribution scenarios requiring segment reallocation. 

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments for penalty and interest rule "CREDIT_INT". 

 

*Non functional requirements*
Performance , Security, Traceability, Accessibility, Usability  DODs should be fulfilled.  | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: Enhance credit interest calculation to include unallocated payment segments, so as to provide an accurate interest calculation.  | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: Calculate *credit* / reimbursement interest for *unallocated credits on a payment segment* (next to credits on bill segments that is already implemented).
IRM: IRM-19514 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: BILLING, ASSESSMENTS AND INSTALLMENTS | Epic: Billing & Assessments Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Add and Maintain Ad-hoc Obligations  Pay Instalment Actions and Categories | Status: HLD | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 880 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Add and Maintain Ad-hoc Obligations  Pay Instalment Actions and Categories | Enriched Jira Features.Description: For Ad-hoc obligations : 
As a revenue official, I want to see that a party in a specific role was, is or is going to be obliged to pay an assessment in instalments, so that I can check whether this party in a specific role is meeting the obligation to pay these instalments on time and in full and can take measures if this is not the case. i.e, I need to be able to add several payment action under an ad-hoc obligations to represent Installments similarly to what is happening in the Periodic Obligations.  
This can be used for Inheritance tax, legacy data migration processes, other cases like Guarantees. 

The goal is to be able to add more than payment obligation actions per obligation for ad-hoc obligations, similarly to what happens with periodic obligations. 

Relevant : [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-11522] , [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-10419]

User can see information that identifies a pay instalment action and its status to the user, such as action category (e.g. preliminary or original), action type, action reference number, action due date, amount and action status (e.g. active or closed).

IRM: IRM-38899 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: TAX ACCOUNTS | Epic: Tax Accounts Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Support Tax Account Overview Page in the Single Taxpayer Overview | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GTM | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 350 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Support Tax Account Overview Page in the Single Taxpayer Overview | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a revenue officer, I want to have an overview of the financial transactions for a revenue type registration that represents a tax account, so that I can see an aggregated, holistic and coherent representation of the financial data of the the tax account in a specificied reconciliation period. 

*Introduction*

This feature describes the functional business requirements for a new single taxpayer overview page within Solon Tax, named the "Tax Account Overview". This new feature will introduce a period-centric overview. It will aggregate and present all financial transactions (FTs) related to a selected _reconciliation period(s)_ for a given revenue type registration, providing an immediate, consolidated view of that period's financial status. 

The purpose of this page is to provide a consolidated view of all Financial Transactions (FTs) associated with a specific reconciliation period for a taxpayer's Tax Account.

Currently, while Solon Tax supports the concept of a Tax Account ({{{}Skattekonto{}}}) and links Financial Transactions to reconciliation periods, there is no dedicated user interface that presents this information in a single, easily accessible view. This feature will bridge that gap, improving visibility and efficiency for Revenue Authority users managing these accounts.

As a reference countries that "Tax Account" is most prevalent in Europe, particularly in Scandinavia and the Nordics, which are global leaders in e-government. 

Currently implementation exists for the "Single Taxpayer Overview" pages, often refered to as 360 View, where a "Taxpayer Financial Overview" exists and can be used as reference. Particularly the last accordion of this page referred as " Financial Details per Financial Transaction". This is a page where all financial transactions for all revenue types are displayed and not only Tax Account that is the scope of this feature. 

*Functional Requirements*
h4. Navigation

A new redirect link shall be introduced on the *Revenue Type Registration (RTR)* page.
 * This link shall only be visible for RTRs that are configured as a "Tax Account" (i.e., where the {{isTaxAccount}} flag on the associated Revenue Type is true).
 * The link will navigate the user to the new "Tax Account Overview" page, passing the context of the current RTR and the selected reconciliation period.
 * Assumption is that the existing link from the party role will continue to function as is with the additional view in scope of this feature for the Tax Account. 

h4. Page Content and Layout

The "Tax Account Overview" page will contain the following elements:
 * *Filters:* User should be able to filter the following information:

 * 
 ** Reconciliation Period Filter
 ** From: 01/01/2026 
 ** To: 31/01/2026 or To: 31/03/2026, meaning more than one reconciliation periods can be selected. 

 
 * *"Update P&I" Button:* User should be able to see and select the "Update P&I" button where he/she can enter the "RECALCULATEFROMDATE" to run Penalty & Interest. 

 * *Financial Transactions Table:* A table displaying all Financial Transactions linked to the selected reconciliation period for the given Tax Account. The table should be read-only and provide standard functionalities like sorting, pagination and Column Configurator. The table should start with an opening balance for the period selected and end with the closing balance. 

Opening Balance of a period should be equal to the closing balance of the previous period. Opening balance should be the running balance of all financial transactions prior to date from selected in the filters. 

Closing Balance of a period is the running balance and should be equal to the Opening of that period plus any financial transaction related to that period such as debts, payments (both allocated and unallocated), interests, write offs, refunds... 

Available Columns (data) for FTs should be:  
 * Creation Date
 * Effective Date (eg. Period Reference - Period the debt/payment refers to)
 * Accounting Date 
 * Origin 
 * FT ID
 * Revenue Type 
 * FT Type 
 * Posting Reason
 * Liability Balance 
 * Running Balance

Please refer to the attached example_updated for a comprehensive view of the Tax Account Overview page.
h3. Assumptions & Dependencies
 * The Revenue Type entity has a configurable attribute to designate it as a "Tax Account."
 * The Financial Transaction entity has an attribute ({{{}reconciliationPeriodCode{}}}) to link it to a specific Reconciliation Period.

*Key features highlighted in this view:*
 * *Opening Balance:* The view starts with the "Opening Balance" showing the tax account's debt from before the selected period.
 * *Running Balance:* A column shows the balance after every single transaction, which is crucial for analysis.
 * *Detailed Descriptions:* Transactions are clearly labeled (e.g., "Payroll Tax Assessment," "Payment Received").
 * *Period Reference:* A column links a transaction back to the original tax period it relates to (e.g., Q4-2025), which is vital for an officer's investigation.

 

*Non functional requirements*
It is expected team to get aligned with respective teams and reassure that is not creating issues or the related NFRs will be tested :
Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability 
DODs should be fulfilled.

More over related to performance the team is expected to provide a solution on how the opening balance will be retrieved considering all past debts. Note that past debts may be related to periods, that may differ per revenue authority, for the last 10 years for example.  | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: This will provide Revenue Authority users with a clear, consolidated view of all financial activities within a specific reconciliation period for a taxpayer's Tax Account, improving efficiency and accuracy. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: * When I am on a revenue type registration for a Tax Account, I can see and click a "View Tax Account Overview" link for that RTR, more details specified in the functional requirements.
 * After clicking the link, I am navigated to a new page titled "Tax Account Overview" for that Tax Account.
 * As a User I am able to filter the from and to reconciliation periods I am interested to see financial transactions for, more details specified in the functional requirements. 
 * User should be able to see in the UI a Table with financial transactions is updated with an opening and closing balance as per attached example_updated and functional requirements in this feature, more details specified in the functional requirements.

IRM: IRM-37845 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: REGISTRATION | Epic: Registration Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Enhance Validity period conditions in Registry detail entities to support multiple modifications in the same date | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 800 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Enhance Validity period conditions in Registry detail entities to support multiple modifications in the same date | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a revenue officer I need to be able to complete several Party details changes in the same date and system will allow this without effecting uniqueness and overlapping checks that are applied to Party and Party Role child entities with valid-from/valid-to periods.

The same logic must also apply when system determines which registry records are considered valid for a specific date (e.g., Today view in the UI or a historical date view).

The solution should be able to support same day changes for : 

a) records with valid-from/valid-to dates are considered duplicated or overlapping.
b) primary records with valid-from/valid-to dates are considered duplicated.
c) The criteria used to determine which records are valid on a specific reference date (current date or historical date).

Child objects to be considered : 
 * {color:#172b4d}Party role{color}
 * {color:#172b4d}party_identifier, party_name{color}
 * Party_state, party_address, party_contact ,Bank account  , Preferences,  party_classification, party additional details
 * {color:#172b4d}party_role_relationship, asset_party_role_relationship, asset_to_asset_relationship, valuation , party role eligible states {color}

Assumption : We assume that the error handing and the exceptions logged as well as the remaining uniqueness validations mechanisms are functional in the product for all registry entities. (Party , Party role, Claimant, User, Organ. Unit, Asset)

 

*Functional requirements*

 

*New Fields* 
 * For all the above mentioned Party child objects, Party , Party Role, add Optional fields 
Valid State? , Boolean 
State Reason, Free text 
 * Make fields searchable
 * Make fields visible in the UI
 * Make fields updatable as/where the Valid from /to fields are
 * Move the information to relevant Party role sections (as Valid from/to) 
 * Default value of valid_state = true (e.g. when creating a record)
 ** All existing records are migrated with valid_state = true
 * (!)   Define if a record type should be checked for uniqueness or not 
Field: Check if unique?  /Boolean

*Rules for Unique record check:*

For the same record type (or per case additional filters are used, such as in Identifiers the country) 
If the record is flagged as Valid
check  if the period is not overlapping other periods 
In case of end date = other records start date then the end date overlapping with other record start date is ignored. (i.e. only end date of one period is the same as the start date of another period, see bullet 4) 
 # If a record  flag Valid? = false : it is ignored during uniqueness checks and for primary checks.
 # If a record  flag CheckifUnique? = false : it is ignored during uniqueness checks and for primary checks.   (!)
 # If a record Start date = End date= Y  , Flag Valid ? = true  : record is selected primary or considered proper entry for date Y   (primary set for start date Y,  if flagged as primary) 
 # If  Record 1 start date end = A  and end date = X  , valid = true
and Record 2 start date = X , end date = B , valid = true
both  flag Valid? = true ,  
Then these records are not considered overlapping (although in current rule are consider overlapping). 
On date X, the valid record is Record2 (the record with start date X)
Not the one with end date = X (Record 1).
 # If Record1: start date is null , end date  = X  , valid = true
Record2: start date  = X , end date  = null  , valid = true
The record 2 is selected primary or the considered for date x 
 # If Record1: start date is null , end date  = null  , valid = true
Record2: start date  = X , end date  = null   , valid = true
 System will not allow this because of overlapping in other days (!)
 # If two records of the same type, 
and both have Valid state = true, 
when their validity periods overlap (e.g. 5) , the system rejects the change due to overlapping validity periods. (!)
 # A record is considered for date D when: 
valid state = true and 
start date <= D  and End date is null or end date > D , valid = true
 # If multiple changes occur in the same transaction, Uniqueness validation must run after final state.
 # Notes:
 ## If valid to = null means infinite validity
 ## API queries using reference dates follow the same validity rules
 ## the  included fields in uniqueness checks already considered (e.g. in Identities the countries, or the type of the record) should continue be used.

 

*Apply to :*
 * Validation of Uniqueness of primary records per period
 * Validation of Uniqueness of records per type (and other flags as per entity) per period
 * Define the visibly records that defines the view of today, history date, date in the past 

*UI :*

 Filter history records by valid from 
 If valid_state = false , state_reason must be populated

Document all the above adjustments.

Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability  DODs should be fulfilled.

IRM: IRM-30362 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: TAXPAYER ACCOUNTING | Epic: Taxpayer Accounting Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: GL decisions table - Ensure extensibility and high volume support of decisions /Functionality & Reference Implementation | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 1600 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: GL decisions table - Ensure extensibility and high volume support of decisions /Functionality & Reference Implementation | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As an administrator responsible for configuring the GL Decision Table (Accountant table), iI need to support the extensibility of the solution. 
I need to introduce additional parameters that control how GL accounts are split across multiple files or tables. This is required to support very high volumes of decision lines and complex business rules.
I need to allow custom adapters to be used on how rules are created and selected to generate journal entries. 

These parameters will allow the system to efficiently handle hundreds of special cases, reduce the size and complexity of individual GL decision tables, and improve maintainability by splitting configurations into multiple, logically grouped records. 

A realistic number of GL decision lines with the assumption that legacy GLs will be removed from time to time, is 200.000 lines

 

*Functional Requirements* 


+*1.* Some suggestions on how to support high volumes of rules:+ 

*A) GL Decision Line Volume Support*
 * Decision rule sheets must support modern XLSX row limits (1,048,576+ rows), not legacy XLS limits (65,536 rows).
 * The system should support the use of multiple decision lines per transaction (multi-lines), where applicable.

*B) Split GL Decision Tables Across Multiple Sheets or Files*
 * As an admin/configurator, I must be able to define and use more than one spreadsheet or files for GL Decision Tables.
 * Splitting must be rule-driven and configurable.

*C) Rule Evaluation Mechanism*

The system must determine which spreadsheet(s) to read based on configured split rules.
One FT may require reading:

A single sheet, or Multiple sheets, depending on customer-defined configuration.
Rule evaluation must be deterministic and transparent (traceable which sheets were evaluated).

 

*D)   Reference Implementation Split Strategies (Examples)*
 * The system should support splitting GL decision tables based on configurable parameters, such as FT Origin, RTR relation with Claimants etc: 
 ** Segment type of Origin  of Financial transactions (ft_origin_cl) , splitting spreadsheets for Bill segments, Payment segments, Allocation Segments. 
One sheet for Segment type = Bill segment, one for Payment Segments, one Allocation Segments
 ** If Claimant related (if the revenue type registration is related to a claimant) 
Use a dedicated spreadsheet containing claimant-specific GL mappings.
i.e., If a revenue type is related to a specific claimant, the system reads only the claimant-specific sheet.
 ** The revenue type, Domain
Certification-related mappings in one sheet. 
All other revenue/tax types in separate sheets.
Additional Parameters as reference implementation in GL Decision Table [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-37721] 
 ** Considerations : Customers may also add a rule, to read for every FT,  2 or more sheets,  as the rules sheet may split per Ledger.   (The system reads from two or more sheets per FT, e.g. one per Ledger.) 
Other cases may include parameters to split on segment type category/subcategory or revenue type details and some of these details may be also captured in data areas.


+2. Expandability+

*E) Customers are able to use custom in process implementation*
Be able to adjust a custom implementation in process to run in order  to create journal entries. Interface (as in allocation) to feed the results in Solon Journal entries

 

*Documentation*

All configuration options, split strategies, and rule evaluation logic must be fully documented.

Documentation must include:
 * Usage and Configuration examples
 * Reference implementations
 * Operational guidelines , Performance considerations

*Non functional requirements*

The solution must maintain or improve the product’s:

*Performance* – large datasets and multi-sheet evaluation must not degrade processing times
*Security* – no exposure of sensitive configuration data
*Accessibility* – configuration screens and documentation must remain accessible
*Usability* – splitting logic must be understandable and maintainable by admins
Additionally:
The team must collaborate with domain specialists to validate the above.

All Definition of Done ({*}DoD{*}) criteria must be met. | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: By enabling configurable splitting of GL Decision Tables across multiple rule-based spreadsheets, administrators can manage high-volume and complex accounting rules more efficiently. This reduces configuration errors, improves performance for large datasets, simplifies maintenance, and allows customers to scale GL logic without hitting structural or technical limits. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: *A) GL Decision Line Volume Support*
 * Decision rule sheets must support modern XLSX row limits (1,048,576+ rows), not legacy XLS limits (65,536 rows).

*B) Split GL Decision Tables Across Multiple Sheets or Files*
 * As an admin/configurator, I must be able to define and use more than one spreadsheet or files for GL Decision Tables.
 * Splitting must be rule-driven and configurable.

IRM: IRM-29430 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: PENALTY & INTEREST | Epic: Penalty & Interest Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Enhance Credit Interest Calculation to include unallocated payment segments | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GTM | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 3200 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Enhance Credit Interest Calculation to include unallocated payment segments | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a revenue authority officer I would like Solon RM to consider in credit interest calculation, all payments received from a taxpayer, both allocated and unallocated, so that final interest calculation is accurate and can be used in relevant processes.  

*Introduction*
This feature was originally introduced for SKV implementation of Reimbursement Interest in [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-15910] the credits from Bill segments are considered in the calculations. To complete this interest calculation, system needs to consider all payment segments as well. 

Moving forward for the implemetation of the Tax Account in Northern countries but also for other implementations, in order to calculate interest accurately all payment segments, allocated and unallocated needs to be considered.  

Update the existing CREDIT_INT PI (Penalty & Interest) rule to calculate reimbursement interest on credit unallocated payment segments for tax account scenarios, ensures taxpayers receive proper interest on all credit amounts.

Currently, the system calculates interest only on bill segment balances. However, when for example liability amendments occur (e.g., reducing a VAT liability from €100 to €80 after a €100 payment has been made), the resulting €20 credit unallocated payment segment does not accrue interest in favor of the taxpayer. This creates an unfair situation where taxpayer funds held by the tax authority do not earn the required interest. 

To enhance understanding of this feature and facilitate analysis tasks please find below a business example as well as business cases where Solon Tax results in unallocated payment segments.

*System Requirements*
 * PI Rule Enhancement: Rule Code = CREDIT_INT (Reimbursement Interest Rule) Enhancement: Update calculation logic to include credit unallocated payment segments (next to credits on bill segments that is already implemented). 

*Business Example*

> Initial State:

VAT Liability: €100 (debit)

Payment Made: €100 (credit)

Result: Liability fully paid, balance = €0

> After Amendment:

Amendment: VAT liability reduced by €20 (becomes €80)

Payment Remains: €100 (unchanged)

Result: €20 credit unallocated payment segment

_Current Behavior:_

Interest calculated only on bill segment balances, thus €20 credit unallocated payment segment earns no interest

_Required Behavior:_

Interest calculated on bill segment balances AND credit unallocated payment segments, thus €20 credit unallocated payment segment earns monthly interest in favor of taxpayer

 

*Example Business Cases resulting in Unallocated Payment Segments*
 # Payment Suspense Scenarios, where for example invalid reference number results to a payment that cannot be allocated to a specific party role.
 # Payment File Processing Errors during automated payment file processing due to for example corrupted payment data or reference number mismatch.
 # Insufficient liability balance for full allocation as per the business example above. 
 # Payment Event State Transitions, when for example re-opening completed payment events where original segments need to be cancelled or payment event re-distribution scenarios requiring segment reallocation. 

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments for penalty and interest rule "CREDIT_INT". 

 

*Non functional requirements*
Performance , Security, Traceability, Accessibility, Usability  DODs should be fulfilled.  | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: Enhance credit interest calculation to include unallocated payment segments, so as to provide an accurate interest calculation.  | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: Calculate *credit* / reimbursement interest for *unallocated credits on a payment segment* (next to credits on bill segments that is already implemented).
IRM: IRM-19514 | Initiative Group: CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | Initiative: BILLING, ASSESSMENTS AND INSTALLMENTS | Epic: Billing & Assessments Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Add and Maintain Ad-hoc Obligations – Pay Instalment Actions and Categories | Status: HLD | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 880 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Add and Maintain Ad-hoc Obligations – Pay Instalment Actions and Categories | Enriched Jira Features.Description: For Ad-hoc obligations : 
As a revenue official, I want to see that a party in a specific role was, is or is going to be obliged to pay an assessment in instalments, so that I can check whether this party in a specific role is meeting the obligation to pay these instalments on time and in full and can take measures if this is not the case. i.e, I need to be able to add several payment action under an ad-hoc obligations to represent Installments similarly to what is happening in the Periodic Obligations.  
This can be used for Inheritance tax, legacy data migration processes, other cases like Guarantees. 

The goal is to be able to add more than payment obligation actions per obligation for ad-hoc obligations, similarly to what happens with periodic obligations. 

Relevant : [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-11522] , [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-10419] 

*Functional Requirements*

*Basics*
 * User and admin can create multiple payment obligation actions under an ad-hoc obligation (revenue type category = Ad-hoc)  as installments, following the structure of the non ad-hoc obligations with installments. 
 ** User can add a Filing and more that one Payment Actions in ad-hoc Obligation, flagged as Installments 
 ** User can define the Category as is in periodic ones : Preliminary, Original
 ** User can define the due date (as happens now)
 ** Status is managed by the system (as happens now). 
 ** One set of actions per category will be permitted and I can add more that one payment actions if type is installment but one if it is once- off,  . I.e., same validations as in periodic ones regarding grouping per category, 
 * User can see the list of pay instalment actions that a party in a specific role -  was, is or is going to be  - obliged to perform for a specific revenue type for a specific revenue period or once-off. User can see information that identifies a pay instalment action and its status to the user, such as action category (e.g. preliminary or original), action type, action reference number, action due date, amount and action status (e.g. active or closed).
 * User can create manually the payment obligation actions (as happens now).
 * User can sort the list.
 * User can open a pay instalment action to see more details and update if needed. 

 

-*Advanced:*- 

-*Additional functionality:*- 
-To be able for the user to create several installments, a set of predefined rules may be ready in a way that  :- 
-User will add some parameters such as already logged start date, due date , will add some additional such as : number of installments,  duration between installments, type of action (payment) to be created and margin to grace date. Will click a button and installments will be created.  Then user will be able to update the entries.- 
 * -Admin can define the rule in the revenue type on how  to create the installments for ad-hoc revenue types (suggestion : Dynamic Rules)- 
 ** -Rules will be able via parameters added by user to generate payment actions under an ad-hoc obligation.-  
 ** -Rule will calculate a) the ad-hoc installments / payment actions :  according set by user start date, duration between installments , number of installments , margin of grace date, category . b) Filing actions according Start date , due date of the obligation, margin of Grace date , category-

-+Consideration+-
-User should be able to define the rule to create the installments (e.g.  Dynamic Rules or batches)- 
-Rules should be able via parameters added by user to generate payment actions under an ad-hoc obligation.-  
-Rule may calculate a) the ad-hoc installments / payment actions :  according set by user start date, duration between installments , number of installments , margin of grace date, category . b) Filing actions according Start date , due date of the obligation, margin of Grace date , category-

 

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments. 

 

*Non functional requirements*
It is expected that the NFRs are considered and examined: Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability 

DODs should be fulfilled.

([https://netcompany.sharepoint.com/sites/NCTMS.GR.LT_TAX/Delte%20dokumenter/Forms/AllItems.aspx?id=%2Fsites%2FNCTMS%2EGR%2ELT%5FTAX%2FDelte%20dokumenter%2F03%2EExecuting%2FImplementation%2FBP03%2FDeliverables&p=true&ga=1)]{color}*

*Background*

Representations are already implemented in the application as . 
In this features
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-4743] 
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-4744]

[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-4746]   {color}{+}(Subusers){+}{color:#172b4d}
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-5026] 
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-32538]   {color}{color:#172b4d}(data areas and support external systems as in LT branch)
Delegations enhancements in [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-38408] {color}

The purpose of this feature is to validate the current implementation based on new requirements and make small adjustments. 

{color:#172b4d}In this feature will name: 
*Requester*            : The user asking someone else to represent them
*Representative*    : The user who may act on behalf of the requester. This user may also ask to be represented.  
2-ways: Both may be initiate a representation request and the other part will reply.
Multilevel: Many levels of representation should be supported. {color}

     *Authorization schema* /Multiple levels of authorizations  (see also delegations with sub-users in [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-38408] )
 * The authorization scheme support  *2-ways.*   
*Requester*  to *Representative*     ,
*Representative* to *Requester*   
 * The authorization scheme support  *multiple levels* of representations. (see sub users :[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-38408] ) 
i.e., several levels of sub-users may be able to be defined. 
{color:#505f79}Examples:  {color}
{color:#505f79}1) The (account and user) *Legal Person* to a user of *Company's legal representative*{color}
{color:#505f79}2) *Company's legal representative*  to an *Accounting firm*  to manage the accountings  of the company{color}
{color:#505f79}3) *Accounting firm* to the user  of  *Accountant employee* to delegate/assign the task{color}
{color:#505f79}or{color}
{color:#505f79}1) A (account and user) *Natural person* to a user of his/her *Guardian* (e.g. father)
2) *Guardian* to an *Accounting firm* 
3) *Accounting firm*  to the *Accounting firm's legal representative*
4) *Accounting firm's legal representative to the*  *Accountant employee*{color}
 * {color:#172b4d}If a representation is delegated, then the delegation may happen with the rights assigned to the main representative or less. Cannot add more rights to delegator. (As-is){color}
 * Admins should be able to view and track the level of representation per Agreement. 

 
----
*Functional requirements*

 

{color:#172b4d}*Configuration*{color}
 * {color:#172b4d}Configurators should be able to define validations for the agreements and levels of agreements (Dependent on [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-38408]  )
(Example :  
Max_depth :  May delegate for up to 3 levels , if Account to user is not count as representation and first representation is level 0 
Non allowed circular representations)  {color}
 * {color:#172b4d}Configurators may *define Agreement types* (Agreement cl) e.g. , Legal Representation , Legal Representation{color}
 * Configurators may *define their own statuses and lifecycle.*
 * Customers may define the default Source system and purpose values (CLs){*}{{*}}

 

*Additional Configuration level*
 * Configurators may define if in SS they need to capture :  agreements, agreement services (as is ) but also the *agreement service rights*  (see LT implementation with new table in ss schema)  to be able to define the rights per agreement service (see [https://netcompany.sharepoint.com/sites/NCTMS.GR.LT_TAX/Delte%20dokumenter/Forms/AllItems.aspx?id=%2Fsites%2FNCTMS%2EGR%2ELT%5FTAX%2FDelte%20dokumenter%2F03%2EExecuting%2FImplementation%2FBP03%2FDeliverables%2FDD120%20%2D%20Physical%20Datamodel&viewid=9186892f%2Df5b0%2D4a0b%2Da210%2D187a381e18c8&p=true)] 

      Considerations: 
 * 
 ** {color:#172b4d}Configurators should be able to define criteria to define the list of allowed representatives
(Example  : If Account = Company , Representative id not the legal company representative can be an Accounting firm or employee of a firm with permission of Books category A) {color}

*Search for users*
 * User search users to be selected for representation only by IDs but cannot see other user details 

*Levels*
 - As a user I may  delegate the representation to another existing user.  The levels of delegation may be *multiple as noted in examples above* .
 - {*}{{*}}{color:#172b4d}As a user  I may see the level of the representation and the representative that assign this to me in the UI.{color} 
 - Lifecycle is maintained for all representation levels.

*Lifecycle Permissions* 
 * Admin, Users and Procedures may log *"Change status reason"* , text  (e.g. revoked reason, cancel reason)  in *Agreements.* 
 * Users and procedures may set the *status* for Agreements. (available field and lifecycle). 
 * ?dmins should be able to view and track the level of representation per Agreement. 
 * Delegated permissions are *equal or less that* representation rights from delegator, i.e. permissions inheritance or remove some rights but cannot add more that already assigned to the delegator.
Representator 1 : Agreement Service 1,  with rights 1,2  ->   Delegated representator 2 : Agreement Service 1,  with rights 1,2 
or
Representator 1 : Agreement Service 1,  with rights 1,2  ->  Delegated representator 2 : Agreement Service 1,  with right 1

In case of some representations as sub users, then needs to follow implementation in  [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-38408] 
 * Permissions on requests forms  may be based on the  Lifecycle. 
for status change, reason may be filled in Optionally (see above field Change status reason{*}){*}  
Status Field is RO  in UI , buttons will manage the flow. 
(e.g. , as is implemented in product) 
 ** 
 *** *Pending* (Temporally save , not applied/committed not considered) -(To avoid incorrect Requester  or representative selected (similar names, wrong identifier).  
Created by *Representative* or  *Requester*  (see above 2-ways and multilevel)
Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** {*}Access Proposed{*}: Requested agreement but not processed
Set by the process  (that was previously initiated by  Representative  or  Requester )
Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** *Access Denied* :   Agreement is not established
 Set by the process/system  because of an error or incorrect selection of representation users or other validation.
Status Field is RO for the users
 Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** *Access Granted :* agreement/representation is valid. (Configured value as the cl value that provides access)   
Set by the process based on what replied  by  Representative  or  Requester (the receiver of the request) 
Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** *Access Revoked :* agreement/representation is not valid any more.
Set by the process based on what replied  by  Representative  or  Requester (the receiver of the request) 
Revoked by process because of end date reached 
Revoked by any part of the agreement 
Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** *Canceled  :* agreement/representation is not valid
Set by the process based on what replied  by  Representative  or  Requester (the receiver of the request) 
Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** After cancel and revoke record cannot change any status.
User need to create a new record to extend this. 

                                     !image-2026-03-10-09-10-29-034.png!

 
 * If in  representation  1->2->3->4  i.e, 1->2 and  2->3 and  3->4  
If  1->2  is canceled then 2->3 ??? 3->4 get canceled 
If 2->3  is canceled then 3->4  is canceled but 1->2 is not. 
Same with revokes. 

 * To be accepted a  representation  1 to 4 (1->2->3->4) there should have been accepted the 1->2 , 2->3, 3->4

 

*Versioning*
 * Changes should be logged in Audit log.

IRM: IRM-36664 | Initiative Group: CORE SELF SERVICE CAPABILITIES | Initiative: USER & 3RD PARTY ACCESS MANAGEMENT | Epic: User & 3rd Party Access Management Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Representations : Define Date time and timezone for Representations and user rights /RM &SS | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 480 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Representations : Define Date time and timezone for Representations and user rights /RM &SS | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As an admin user, I need to capture and manage Start Date and End Date fields in the system that define the validity period of granted permissions, so that access rights can be controlled accurately and limited to specific timeframes.

*Functional requirements*

*Basics:* 
 * Start and End date are captured as datetime and properly defined time zone in Agreements.
 * Start and End date are captured as datetime and properly defined time zone in Agreements services.
 * Start and End date are captured as datetime and properly defined time zone in user rights.
 * The permissions should be enforced or recalled in datetime level.  (along status define in [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-36665]) 
 * If no end date is defined the system should clearly flag in UI  "No End Date

Note: Already available fields in Party role relationship.

*Timezone* 
 * Display datetime in the users configured timezone.
 * Validity must be calculated based on stored system time (not client browser time).
 * Daylight Saving Time (DST) transitions must not cause early expiration or extended validity.

*Versioning*
 * Changes should be logged in Audit log.

*Validations* 
 * End Date cannot be earlier than Start Date.
 * Start Date is mandatory.

IRM: IRM-36660 | Initiative Group: CORE SELF SERVICE CAPABILITIES | Initiative: SELF SERVICE SERVICES MANAGEMENT | Epic: Self Service Services Management Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Attachments in Forms - Document Uploads enhancements before and after saving the form / RM & SS | Status: In Design | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 792 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Attachments in Forms - Document Uploads enhancements before and after saving the form / RM & SS | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a taxpayer or revenue authority user, I want to upload and manage required attachments while filling in a form (even before saving it), including during registration forms where the relevant party is not yet created, so that I can complete the submission process without unnecessary interruptions. 

*Background*
In as-is system the form should be saved in order to be able to upload documents.

*Functional Requirements*
 * Users (revenue officer or taxpayer) can upload attachments with permitted metadata while filling the form, before saving.

 * Users can view the list of uploaded attachments while filling the form (before saving).

 * Before and After saving, users can:
View attachments
Add new attachments
Remove attachments
Edit metadata
 * In RM , users can link attachments to additional system records (e.g., case file) while managing form attachments.

 * If attachment upload fails:
The user is clearly informed by a message that attachment was not successfully uploaded. 
Form saving/submission is not blocked.
Successfully uploaded files remain attached. (Orphan issue).  

 * Attachments modifications after saving are stored in audit log

will result in a better UX as it provides form filing steps clarity,  fewer "incomplete" submissions, delays because of missing attachments, and higher data integrity by ensuring documents are linked directly to the relevant parties/roles at the point of entry.
A measurement of filling form decrease time may be useful.  | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: # Upload Before Save : User is  able to upload an attachments filling all applicable metadata while creating a form.

 # Failure Handling : Message appears if upload is failed without interrupting the form saving.

IRM: IRM-36665 | Initiative Group: CORE SELF SERVICE CAPABILITIES | Initiative: USER & 3RD PARTY ACCESS MANAGEMENT | Epic: User & 3rd Party Access Management Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Representations : (A) Enhancements, configurability and permissions in Agreements (2ways,multilevels)  /RM & SS   | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 480 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Representations : (A) Enhancements, configurability and permissions in Agreements (2ways,multilevels)  /RM & SS   | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As an admin user, 
I need to capture the status, source system and integration time of representations defined as to be able to know how the representations were created.
Representations are 2-ways authorized. 
Representations are multilevels
A lifecycle should be defined to representations forms as to be able to temporally saved, validated and revoked. 

*{color:#ff8b00}CHECK ! Review the LT branch for any implemented functionalities that can be merged into the product. ([https://netcompany.sharepoint.com/sites/NCTMS.GR.LT_TAX/Delte%20dokumenter/Forms/AllItems.aspx?id=%2Fsites%2FNCTMS%2EGR%2ELT%5FTAX%2FDelte%20dokumenter%2F03%2EExecuting%2FImplementation%2FBP03%2FDeliverables&p=true&ga=1)]{color}*

*Background*

Representations are already implemented in the application as . 
In this features
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-4743] 
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-4744]
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-4745] (Subusers)
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-4746]   {color}{+}(Subusers){+}{color:#172b4d}
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-5026] 
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-32538]   {color}{color:#172b4d}(data areas and support external systems as in LT branch)
Delegations enhancements in [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-38408] {color}

The purpose of this feature is to validate the current implementation based on new requirements and make small adjustments. 

{color:#172b4d}In this feature will name: 
*Requester*            : The user asking someone else to represent them
*Representative*    : The user who may act on behalf of the requester. This user may also ask to be represented.  
2-ways: Both may be initiate a representation request and the other part will reply.
Multilevel: Many levels of representation should be supported. {color}

     *Authorization schema* /Multiple levels of authorizations  (see also delegations with sub-users in [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-38408] )
 * The authorization scheme support  *2-ways.*   
*Requester*  to *Representative*     ,
*Representative* to *Requester*   
 * The authorization scheme support  *multiple levels* of representations. (see sub users :[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-38408] ) 
i.e., several levels of sub-users may be able to be defined. 
{color:#505f79}Examples:  {color}
{color:#505f79}1) The (account and user) *Legal Person* to a user of *Company's legal representative*{color}
{color:#505f79}2) *Company's legal representative*  to an *Accounting firm*  to manage the accountings  of the company{color}
{color:#505f79}3) *Accounting firm* to the user  of  *Accountant employee* to delegate/assign the task{color}
{color:#505f79}or{color}
{color:#505f79}1) A (account and user) *Natural person* to a user of his/her *Guardian* (e.g. father)
2) *Guardian* to an *Accounting firm* 
3) *Accounting firm*  to the *Accounting firm's legal representative*
4) *Accounting firm's legal representative to the*  *Accountant employee*{color}
 * {color:#172b4d}If a representation is delegated, then the delegation may happen with the rights assigned to the main representative or less. Cannot add more rights to delegator. (As-is){color}
 * Admins should be able to view and track the level of representation per Agreement. 

 
----
*Functional requirements*

 

{color:#172b4d}*Configuration*{color}
 * {color:#172b4d}Configurators should be able to define validations for the agreements and levels of agreements (Dependent on [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-38408]  )
(Example :  
Max_depth :  May delegate for up to 3 levels , if Account to user is not count as representation and first representation is level 0 
Non allowed circular representations)  {color}
 * {color:#172b4d}Configurators may *define Agreement types* (Agreement cl) e.g. , Legal Representation , Legal Representation{color}
 * Configurators may *define their own statuses and lifecycle.*
 * Customers may define the default Source system and purpose values (CLs){*}{{*}}

 

*Additional Configuration level*
 * Configurators may define if in SS they need to capture :  agreements, agreement services (as is ) but also the *agreement service rights*  (see LT implementation with new table in ss schema)  to be able to define the rights per agreement service (see [https://netcompany.sharepoint.com/sites/NCTMS.GR.LT_TAX/Delte%20dokumenter/Forms/AllItems.aspx?id=%2Fsites%2FNCTMS%2EGR%2ELT%5FTAX%2FDelte%20dokumenter%2F03%2EExecuting%2FImplementation%2FBP03%2FDeliverables%2FDD120%20%2D%20Physical%20Datamodel&viewid=9186892f%2Df5b0%2D4a0b%2Da210%2D187a381e18c8&p=true)] 

      Considerations: 
 * 
 ** {color:#172b4d}Configurators should be able to define criteria to define the list of allowed representatives
(Example  : If Account = Company , Representative id not the legal company representative can be an Accounting firm or employee of a firm with permission of Books category A) {color}

*Search for users*
 * User search users to be selected for representation only by IDs but cannot see other user details 

*Levels*
 - As a user I may  delegate the representation to another existing user.  The levels of delegation may be *multiple as noted in examples above* .
 - {*}{{*}}{color:#172b4d}As a user  I may see the level of the representation and the representative that assign this to me in the UI.{color} 
 - Lifecycle is maintained for all representation levels.

*Lifecycle Permissions* 
 * Admin, Users and Procedures may log *"Change status reason"* , text  (e.g. revoked reason, cancel reason)  in *Agreements.* 
 * Users and procedures may set the *status* for Agreements. (available field and lifecycle). 
 * Αdmins should be able to view and track the level of representation per Agreement. 
 * Delegated permissions are *equal or less that* representation rights from delegator, i.e. permissions inheritance or remove some rights but cannot add more that already assigned to the delegator.
Representator 1 : Agreement Service 1,  with rights 1,2  ->   Delegated representator 2 : Agreement Service 1,  with rights 1,2 
or
Representator 1 : Agreement Service 1,  with rights 1,2  ->  Delegated representator 2 : Agreement Service 1,  with right 1

In case of some representations as sub users, then needs to follow implementation in  [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-38408] 
 * Permissions on requests forms  may be based on the  Lifecycle. 
for status change, reason may be filled in Optionally (see above field Change status reason{*}){*}  
Status Field is RO  in UI , buttons will manage the flow. 
(e.g. , as is implemented in product) 
 ** 
 *** *Pending* (Temporally save , not applied/committed not considered) -(To avoid incorrect Requester  or representative selected (similar names, wrong identifier).  
Created by *Representative* or  *Requester*  (see above 2-ways and multilevel)
Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** {*}Access Proposed{*}: Requested agreement but not processed
Set by the process  (that was previously initiated by  Representative  or  Requester )
Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** *Access Denied* :   Agreement is not established
 Set by the process/system  because of an error or incorrect selection of representation users or other validation.
Status Field is RO for the users
 Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** *Access Granted :* agreement/representation is valid. (Configured value as the cl value that provides access)   
Set by the process based on what replied  by  Representative  or  Requester (the receiver of the request) 
Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** *Access Revoked :* agreement/representation is not valid any more.
Set by the process based on what replied  by  Representative  or  Requester (the receiver of the request) 
Revoked by process because of end date reached 
Revoked by any part of the agreement 
Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** *Canceled  :* agreement/representation is not valid
Set by the process based on what replied  by  Representative  or  Requester (the receiver of the request) 
Set by Admin in SS/RM

 * 
 ** 
 *** After cancel and revoke record cannot change any status.
User need to create a new record to extend this. 

                                     !image-2026-03-10-09-10-29-034.png!

 
 * If in  representation  1->2->3->4  i.e, 1->2 and  2->3 and  3->4  
If  1->2  is canceled then 2->3 και 3->4 get canceled 
If 2->3  is canceled then 3->4  is canceled but 1->2 is not. 
Same with revokes. 

 * To be accepted a  representation  1 to 4 (1->2->3->4) there should have been accepted the 1->2 , 2->3, 3->4

 

*Versioning*
 * Changes should be logged in Audit log.
