IRM: IRM-36664 | Initiative Group: CORE SELF SERVICE CAPABILITIES | Initiative: USER & 3RD PARTY ACCESS MANAGEMENT | Epic: User & 3rd Party Access Management Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Representations : Define Date time and timezone for Representations and user rights /RM &SS | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 480 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Representations : Define Date time and timezone for Representations and user rights /RM &SS | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As an admin user, I need to capture and manage Start Date and End Date fields in the system that define the validity period of granted permissions, so that access rights can be controlled accurately and limited to specific timeframes.

*{color:#ff8b00}CHECK ! Review the LT branch for any implemented functionalities that can be merged into the product.{color}*

*Functional requirements*

*Basics:* 
 * Start and End date are captured as datetime and properly defined time zone in Agreements.
 * Start and End date are captured as datetime and properly defined time zone in Agreements services.
 * Start and End date are captured as datetime and properly defined time zone in user rights.
 * The permissions should be enforced or recalled in datetime level.  (along status define in [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-36665]) 
 * If no end date is defined the system should clearly flag in UI  "No End Date”

Note: Already available fields in Party role relationship.

*Timezone* 
 * Display datetime in the user’s configured timezone.
 * Validity must be calculated based on stored system time (not client browser time).
 * Daylight Saving Time (DST) transitions must not cause early expiration or extended validity.

*Versioning*
 * Changes should be logged in Audit log.

*Validations* 
 * End Date cannot be earlier than Start Date.
 * Start Date is mandatory.

Document all the above adjustments.

IRM: IRM-36660 | Initiative Group: CORE SELF SERVICE CAPABILITIES | Initiative: SELF SERVICE SERVICES MANAGEMENT | Epic: Self Service Services Management Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Attachments in Forms - Document Uploads enhancements before and after saving the form / RM & SS | Status: In Design | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 792 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Attachments in Forms - Document Uploads enhancements before and after saving the form / RM & SS | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a taxpayer or revenue authority user, I want to upload and manage required attachments while filling in a form (even before saving it), including during registration forms where the relevant party is not yet created, so that I can complete the submission process without unnecessary interruptions. 

*Background*
In as-is system the form should be saved in order to be able to upload documents.

*Functional Requirements*
 * Users (revenue officer or taxpayer) can upload attachments with permitted metadata while filling the form, before saving.

 * Users can view the list of uploaded attachments while filling the form (before saving).

 * Before and After saving, users can:
View attachments
Add new attachments
Remove attachments
Edit metadata
 * In RM , users can link attachments to additional system records (e.g., case file) while managing form attachments.

 * If attachment upload fails:
The user is clearly informed by a message that attachment was not successfully uploaded. 
Form saving/submission is not blocked.
Successfully uploaded files remain attached. (Orphan issue).  

 * Attachments modifications after saving are stored in audit log

 

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments. 

*Non functional requirements*
It is expected team to get aligned with respective teams and reassure that is not creating issues or the related NFRs will be tested :
Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability 
DODs should be fulfilled. | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: We believe that allowing users to upload and manage attachments during the form-filling process (pre-save)
will result in a better UX as it provides form filing steps clarity,  fewer "incomplete" submissions, delays because of missing attachments, and higher data integrity by ensuring documents are linked directly to the relevant parties/roles at the point of entry.
A measurement of filling form decrease time may be useful.  | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: # Upload Before Save : User is  able to upload an attachments filling all applicable metadata while creating a form.
 # View and Manage Attachments Before and After Save:  user is able to see and manage attachments before and after saving form. After saving in RM user may additional link attachments to other records.
 # Failure Handling : Message appears if upload is failed without interrupting the form saving.
 # Post-Save Management: user shall have the ability to add new attachments or update the metadata of existing ones, with all changes logged in the system audit trail.

IRM: IRM-38682 | Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Initiative: UI CONFIGURATION | Epic: UI Configuration Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: UI/UX Improvements : Prefilling a field in a form based on the value of another field | Status: Waiting Solution Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 160 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: UI/UX Improvements : Prefilling a field in a form based on the value of another field | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a user I need when a codelist is mandatory and only one item is available and no default value , system to autofill the existing value. 

As a user I need when 2 codelist  1 (parent) , 2 (child) via codelist items are related (e.g.   codelist 1, A item  -as parent - ,  when selected,  result to codelist 2,  B item - as child  ) and user selects parent value A when for B only the value B is available , the value b to be auto selected and prefilled. 

As a configurator I need to be able to set in the codelists an optional to be used  attribute , that may instruct  the prefill  of codelist item value in this codelists, if one value is available based on filters.

*Functional requirements*

Configurator may set in codelist fields an optionally used attribute/metadato , e.g. "AutofillIfUnique"
which attribute will enable in UI the autofill of value in codelist, when only one  codelist item value is available based on filters and related codelist items.
 * Examples/ Cases : 
 ** +Mandatory items case+
In a Mandatory Codelist "C3"  , Non default value is defined 
The only available value is the "C Value" 
When use this field in forms, autoselect and prefil "C Value". 
 ** +Related codelist items case+
Codelist "C1 parent"  ,  Values A1, A2 
Codelist "C2 child"  ,  Values B1, B2 , B3
Relations : 
C1 parent  -> A1 with  C2 child -> B2 (ONLY) 
user selects A1 
Autoselect and prefil B2  value in C2 

 

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments.

IRM: IRM-38250 | Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Initiative: REFERENCE DATA | Epic: Reference Data Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Enhance codelist items codes flexibility and historical track in Solon Tax | Status: In Design | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 560 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Enhance codelist items codes flexibility and historical track in Solon Tax | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As an RM Admin, I can update reference data with a codelist item having a code that is not unique, while its description is updated with different validity periods (no overlap), so as to comply with EU regulating updates.

*Introduction* 

*Tax Activity Codes in the EU:* There is no single "tax code" for all EU members. Instead, three main systems are used:
 * {*}NACE Codes{*}: The official statistical classification for economic activities. The current version is *NACE Rev. 2.1* (effective Jan 1, 2025). Attached in this feature for reference. 
 * {*}VAT Category Codes{*}: Standardized letters (e.g., *S* for Standard, *E* for Exempt) used in electronic invoicing.
 * {*}VATEX Codes{*}: Specific codes used to justify *VAT exemptions* based on EU Directive 2006/112/EC.
 * *Customs Codes (TARIC/CN)* For the import/export of goods, the Combined Nomenclature (CN) is used, which is an 8-digit coding system. 

In Greece, AADE (Independent Authority for Public Revenue) has proceeded with the mapping of the old activity codes (KAD 2008) to the new KAD 2025, a process which began on March 1, 2026. There is a direct correlation between Greek KAD (Activity Code Numbers) and NACE codes. KAD constitute the national version of the European NACE classification.
 * {*}Structure{*}: The first 4 characters of an eight-digit Greek KAD are fully identical to the 4 characters of the corresponding NACE code.
 * {*}2026 Harmonization{*}: AADE recently proceeded (as of 01/03/2026) with an automatic update of KADs for 1.9 million Tax IDs (AFM), in order to fully harmonize them with the new European standard {*}NACE Rev. 2.1{*}.
 * {*}Purpose{*}: This mapping ensures that economic activities in Greece are comparable to those of other EU member states for statistical and regulatory purposes.

*When a Code is Updated*

When the EU updates the NACE structure:
 * {*}Automatic Migration{*}: Most codes are automatically updated by national tax authorities (like AADE in Greece) if there is a 1-to-1 match.
 * {*}Manual Selection{*}: If one old code splits into multiple new ones, the taxpayer must manually select the most accurate one via the tax portal.
 * {*}Description Changes{*}: A code's number *can stay the same while its description* *is updated* to reflect modern technology or clearer definitions.

Validity and History
 * {*}Historical Accuracy{*}: A code must be valid for the period it was used. If you are filing an amended return for 2024, you use the code that was active in 2024, not the new 2025/2026 version.
 * {*}EU-Wide Validity{*}: This principle of historicity applies to all EU countries. While the digital portals differ (e.g., myAADE in Greece), the transition logic to NACE Rev. 2.1 is harmonized across the Union.

For Greek Tax Authority
The code *must remain valid* for the period prior to the change, as tax and statistical representation follows the principle of historicity. In practice, this means the following: * {*}Principle of Historicity{*}: For any transaction, declaration, or audit concerning the past (e.g., fiscal year 2024), the code that was in effect *at that time* is used. New codes (e.g., KAD 2025/2026) apply only to actions from their effective date onwards.
 * {*}System Maintenance{*}: AADE and Eurostat systems maintain the "historical versions" of the codes. If you need to file an amended return for a previous year, you must use the old code that corresponded to that specific period.
 * {*}Migration (Mapping){*}: The mapping performed by AADE does not "erase" the past; it creates a new entry in your Registry history. The "Registry Certificate" will show the expiration date of the old code and the start date of the new one.
 * {*}Audits and Cross-checks{*}: In the event of a tax audit for a past fiscal year, auditors examine the activity based on the description and the code that were in effect at the time of the transaction.

The current Solon Tax platform implementation requires unique codes for codelist items within the same codelist. However, EU tax regulations, particularly for tax activity codes (NACE, VAT Category, VATEX), require the ability to maintain the same code with different descriptions across different validity periods to support historical accuracy and regulatory compliance.

*Current Implementation Support*

The platform currently supports:
 * Unique code constraint for codelist items within a codelist
 * Basic validity period management with valid_from and valid_to fields
 * Codelist item labels with language support

*To Be Implementation*

Allow the same code to be added for different validity periods with:
 * No overlap between validity periods for the same code
 * Different descriptions for the same code across different time periods
 * Historical data preservation for reporting and backdated updates

*Functional Business Requirements*
 # {*}Historical Code Management{*}: Enable codelist items to have the same code with different descriptions across non-overlapping validity periods
 # {*}Temporal Data Integrity{*}: Ensure no validity period overlaps exist for items with the same code within a codelist
 # {*}Backdated Processing Support{*}: Allow selection of historical codelist items when processing backdated taxpayer updates
 # {*}Regulatory Compliance{*}: Support EU tax code evolution requirements (NACE Rev. 2.1)
 # {*}Reporting Continuity{*}: Maintain historical reference data for accurate reporting across different time periods

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments for updating reference data to support compliance with EU updates codes not unique per validity period.

 

*Non functional requirements*
Performance , Security, Traceability, Accessibility, Usability  DODs should be fulfilled.  | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: This enhancement will enable accurate historical tax processing and compliance with EU regulations that require code evolution while maintaining historical accuracy for reporting and backdated transactions. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: * Same codelist item code can exist multiple times with different validity periods (no overlap)
 * Different descriptions can be associated with the same code across different time periods
 * Historical codelist items are preserved and accessible for reporting
 * Backdated taxpayer updates can select appropriate historical codelist items based on transaction date
 * System validates no overlapping validity periods for same code within a codelist
 * Migration functionality supports automatic code updates when 1-to-1 mapping exists
 * Manual selection interface available when one code splits into multiple new codes
 * API endpoints support querying codelist items by effective date
 * UI displays historical versions of codelist items appropriately
IRM: IRM-36668 | Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Initiative: DOCUMENT MANAGEMENT INTEGRATION | Epic: Document Management Integration Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Digital Signatures - System digital signing of PDF documents generated by bpmn process | Status: In Design | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 1440 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Digital Signatures - System digital signing of PDF documents generated by bpmn process | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a revenue authority user, when the system generates a document (e.g., operational reports, letters, certificates) and the business process instructs so, I want the document to be digitally signed by the system, with all required visual elements rendered in the PDF, so that I can securely distribute officially signed documents to taxpayers and stakeholders.

This capability must be reusable, configurable, auditable, and resilient to failures.

*Background :*
In the current (as-is) systems:
Documents are generated via operational reports 
Documents may be instructed to be generated via BPMN flows.
Documents may be sent to contacts and/or stored as attachments. 
Attachments can be linked to a Document Management System (DMS) via integration.

*Assumptions :* 
*a)* Revenue authority will supplied by an External provider the digital stamp (??????? ????????) in ??? or PKC#7 files
Then the configurations for digital signs and certificate will be used for documents signature. 
./pdf_sign_pem_multicert <input_pdf> <output_pdf> <cert.pem> <key.pem>

for our tests we need to use one from CA authority 
*b)* Any additional elements (document IDs, DMS URLs, QR codes) must be printed on the document via project-specific implementation.
{*}c){*}Attachments are integrated with a DMS per customer configuration and responsibility.
*d)* One reference configuration for one digital signature will be only will be available for testing purposes (as demo). If projects needs several signatures, they may be able to configure them in the system.  

*Out of Scope* (for now)
End-user personal digital signatures
Non-PDF document formats
Additional IDs or other document additional elements other than digital signature. (document ID, qr code)

 

 

*Functional Requirements*

*Digital Signature service* 
 * Documents can be digitally signed when instructed by a step in a BPMN flow.
 * The system must expose an API or internal service or other method  for digital signing that can be called by bpmn processes.
 * The signing service must support the signature based on customers configurations and certificate.
 * Admin may configure several signatures.  (May be able to use more than one configurations and certificate / different signatures and bpmn process should decide on which configurations and certificate to be used, but will not be any defaults available in the product).  
 * Keep Audit log for the documents' updates.

*PDF* 
 * The digital signature must be embedded in the PDF according to industry standards (e.g., PAdES).
 * The PDF must remain verifiable by standard PDF readers.

*Storage & Metadata*
 * Signed documents must be stored as attachments  (expected as per relevant integration to be synchronized with the DMS).

 * Document generated is expected to be displayed with  the relevant signature stamp and document ID  (by a reserve id method optionally to be used  in the upload  and that may be used if  needed by configurators) 

*Visual Elements on Document*
Signed documents must display a visible digital signature stamp.

*Unhappy path :*
 * Errors must be logged and be visible.   
 ** Exceptions should be thrown if document generation or digital signature process not completed successfully. 
examples: Document generation fails, Template not found, Missing parameters, Digital signing fails, Timeouts

 

*Reference implementation:* 
 * At the end of the Busreg form, generate a document (operational report)  with all the details filled  per sections same as tabs
Document will be digital signed and stored in attachments linked to the form 
Consideration: Create the signature as a reusable subflow

Timestamp
Document ID
Certificate used

+Configurability+
Be able to select different configurations for digital signs  to be used.

 -LT:- 
|-Every document, whether incoming or system-generated (e.g. forms, letters), must receive a unique registration number.-
-Forms are documents, so forms submitted by users must also have metadata as below:.-|
||-Field-||-Description-||
|-*Document Name*-|-Human-readable title-|
|-*Creator / Author*-|-User or system module creating the document-|
|-*Sender / Receiver*-| * -For sent docs: add recipient.-
 * -For received docs: record sender, their reg. number, original date/title.-|
|-*Date*-|-Created and registered timestamps, YYYY-MM-DD-|
|-*Registration Number*-|-MAP automatically assigns a unique document registration number with a prefix and yearly resetting counter (e.g., 2025-IN-0001, 2025-OUT-0002).-|
|-*Original Document Ref.*-|-Links to the original document (e.g. response to request)-|

IRM: IRM-38250 | Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Initiative: REFERENCE DATA | Epic: Reference Data Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Enhance codelist items codes flexibility and historical track in Solon Tax | Status: In Design | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 560 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Enhance codelist items codes flexibility and historical track in Solon Tax | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As an RM Admin, I can update reference data with a codelist item having a code that is not unique, while its description is updated with different validity periods (no overlap), so as to comply with EU regulating updates.

*Introduction* 

*Tax Activity Codes in the EU:* There is no single "tax code" for all EU members. Instead, three main systems are used:
 * {*}NACE Codes{*}: The official statistical classification for economic activities. The current version is *NACE Rev. 2.1* (effective Jan 1, 2025). Attached in this feature for reference. 
 * {*}VAT Category Codes{*}: Standardized letters (e.g., *S* for Standard, *E* for Exempt) used in electronic invoicing.
 * {*}VATEX Codes{*}: Specific codes used to justify *VAT exemptions* based on EU Directive 2006/112/EC.
 * *Customs Codes (TARIC/CN)* For the import/export of goods, the Combined Nomenclature (CN) is used, which is an 8-digit coding system. 

In Greece, AADE (Independent Authority for Public Revenue) has proceeded with the mapping of the old activity codes (KAD 2008) to the new KAD 2025, a process which began on March 1, 2026. There is a direct correlation between Greek KAD (Activity Code Numbers) and NACE codes. KAD constitute the national version of the European NACE classification.
 * {*}Structure{*}: The first 4 characters of an eight-digit Greek KAD are fully identical to the 4 characters of the corresponding NACE code.
 * {*}2026 Harmonization{*}: AADE recently proceeded (as of 01/03/2026) with an automatic update of KADs for 1.9 million Tax IDs (AFM), in order to fully harmonize them with the new European standard {*}NACE Rev. 2.1{*}.
 * {*}Purpose{*}: This mapping ensures that economic activities in Greece are comparable to those of other EU member states for statistical and regulatory purposes.

*When a Code is Updated*

When the EU updates the NACE structure:
 * {*}Automatic Migration{*}: Most codes are automatically updated by national tax authorities (like AADE in Greece) if there is a 1-to-1 match.
 * {*}Manual Selection{*}: If one old code splits into multiple new ones, the taxpayer must manually select the most accurate one via the tax portal.
 * {*}Description Changes{*}: A code's number *can stay the same while its description* *is updated* to reflect modern technology or clearer definitions.

Validity and History
 * {*}Historical Accuracy{*}: A code must be valid for the period it was used. If you are filing an amended return for 2024, you use the code that was active in 2024, not the new 2025/2026 version.
 * {*}EU-Wide Validity{*}: This principle of historicity applies to all EU countries. While the digital portals differ (e.g., myAADE in Greece), the transition logic to NACE Rev. 2.1 is harmonized across the Union.

For Greek Tax Authority
The code *must remain valid* for the period prior to the change, as tax and statistical representation follows the principle of historicity. In practice, this means the following: * {*}Principle of Historicity{*}: For any transaction, declaration, or audit concerning the past (e.g., fiscal year 2024), the code that was in effect *at that time* is used. New codes (e.g., KAD 2025/2026) apply only to actions from their effective date onwards.
 * {*}System Maintenance{*}: AADE and Eurostat systems maintain the "historical versions" of the codes. If you need to file an amended return for a previous year, you must use the old code that corresponded to that specific period.
 * {*}Migration (Mapping){*}: The mapping performed by AADE does not "erase" the past; it creates a new entry in your Registry history. The "Registry Certificate" will show the expiration date of the old code and the start date of the new one.
 * {*}Audits and Cross-checks{*}: In the event of a tax audit for a past fiscal year, auditors examine the activity based on the description and the code that were in effect at the time of the transaction.

The current Solon Tax platform implementation requires unique codes for codelist items within the same codelist. However, EU tax regulations, particularly for tax activity codes (NACE, VAT Category, VATEX), require the ability to maintain the same code with different descriptions across different validity periods to support historical accuracy and regulatory compliance.

*Current Implementation Support*

The platform currently supports:
 * Unique code constraint for codelist items within a codelist
 * Basic validity period management with valid_from and valid_to fields
 * Codelist item labels with language support

*To Be Implementation*

Allow the same code to be added for different validity periods with:
 * No overlap between validity periods for the same code
 * Different descriptions for the same code across different time periods
 * Historical data preservation for reporting and backdated updates

*Functional Business Requirements*
 # {*}Historical Code Management{*}: Enable codelist items to have the same code with different descriptions across non-overlapping validity periods
 # {*}Temporal Data Integrity{*}: Ensure no validity period overlaps exist for items with the same code within a codelist
 # {*}Backdated Processing Support{*}: Allow selection of historical codelist items when processing backdated taxpayer updates
 # {*}Regulatory Compliance{*}: Support EU tax code evolution requirements (NACE Rev. 2.1)
 # {*}Reporting Continuity{*}: Maintain historical reference data for accurate reporting across different time periods

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments for updating reference data to support compliance with EU updates codes not unique per validity period.

 

*Non functional requirements*
Performance , Security, Traceability, Accessibility, Usability  DODs should be fulfilled.  | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: This enhancement will enable accurate historical tax processing and compliance with EU regulations that require code evolution while maintaining historical accuracy for reporting and backdated transactions. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: * Same codelist item code can exist multiple times with different validity periods (no overlap)
 * Different descriptions can be associated with the same code across different time periods
 * Historical codelist items are preserved and accessible for reporting
 * Backdated taxpayer updates can select appropriate historical codelist items based on transaction date
 * System validates no overlapping validity periods for same code within a codelist
 * Migration functionality supports automatic code updates when 1-to-1 mapping exists
 * Manual selection interface available when one code splits into multiple new codes
 * API endpoints support querying codelist items by effective date
 * UI displays historical versions of codelist items appropriately
IRM: IRM-36668 | Initiative Group: CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | Initiative: DOCUMENT MANAGEMENT INTEGRATION | Epic: Document Management Integration Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Digital Signatures - System digital signing of PDF documents generated by bpmn process | Status: In Design | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 1440 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Digital Signatures - System digital signing of PDF documents generated by bpmn process | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a revenue authority user, when the system generates a document (e.g., operational reports, letters, certificates) and the business process instructs so, I want the document to be digitally signed by the system, with all required visual elements rendered in the PDF, so that I can securely distribute officially signed documents to taxpayers and stakeholders.

This capability must be reusable, configurable, auditable, and resilient to failures.

*Background :*
In the current (as-is) systems:
Documents are generated via operational reports 
Documents may be instructed to be generated via BPMN flows.
Documents may be sent to contacts and/or stored as attachments. 
Attachments can be linked to a Document Management System (DMS) via integration.

*Assumptions :* 
*a)* Revenue authority will supplied by an External provider the digital stamp (ψηφιακή σφραγίδα) in ΡΕΜ or PKC#7 files
Then the configurations for digital signs and certificate will be used for documents signature. 
./pdf_sign_pem_multicert <input_pdf> <output_pdf> <cert.pem> <key.pem>

for our tests we need to use one from CA authority 
*b)* Any additional elements (document IDs, DMS URLs, QR codes) must be printed on the document via project-specific implementation.
{*}c){*}Attachments are integrated with a DMS per customer configuration and responsibility.
*d)* One reference configuration for one digital signature will be only will be available for testing purposes (as demo). If projects needs several signatures, they may be able to configure them in the system.  

*Out of Scope* (for now)
End-user personal digital signatures
Non-PDF document formats
Additional IDs or other document additional elements other than digital signature. (document ID, qr code)

 

 

*Functional Requirements*

*Digital Signature service* 
 * Documents can be digitally signed when instructed by a step in a BPMN flow.
 * The system must expose an API or internal service or other method  for digital signing that can be called by bpmn processes.
 * The signing service must support the signature based on customers configurations and certificate.
 * Admin may configure several signatures.  (May be able to use more than one configurations and certificate / different signatures and bpmn process should decide on which configurations and certificate to be used, but will not be any defaults available in the product).  
 * Keep Audit log for the documents' updates.

*PDF* 
 * The digital signature must be embedded in the PDF according to industry standards (e.g., PAdES).
 * The PDF must remain verifiable by standard PDF readers.

*Storage & Metadata*
 * Signed documents must be stored as attachments  (expected as per relevant integration to be synchronized with the DMS).

 * Document generated is expected to be displayed with  the relevant signature stamp and document ID  (by a reserve id method optionally to be used  in the upload  and that may be used if  needed by configurators) 

*Visual Elements on Document*
Signed documents must display a visible digital signature stamp.

*Unhappy path :*
 * Errors must be logged and be visible.   
 ** Exceptions should be thrown if document generation or digital signature process not completed successfully. 
examples: Document generation fails, Template not found, Missing parameters, Digital signing fails, Timeouts

 

*Reference implementation:* 
 * At the end of the Busreg form, generate a document (operational report)  with all the details filled  per sections same as tabs
Document will be digital signed and stored in attachments linked to the form 
Consideration: Create the signature as a reusable subflow

*Non functional requirements*
It is expected team to get aligned with respective teams and reassure that is not creating issues or the related NFRs will be tested :
Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability 
DODs should be fulfilled.

+Security+
Certificates and private keys must be stored securely (e.g., HSM, secure vault, encrypted storage) or other repository. 
Access to signing functionality must be restricted and auditable.

+Auditability+
Every signing action must be logged:
Who/what triggered the signing
Timestamp
Document ID
Certificate used

+Performance+
Signing should not block critical user flows beyond acceptable SLA limits.
Support async signing for large documents or batch processing.

+Configurability+
Be able to select different configurations for digital signs  to be used.

 -LT:- 
|-Every document, whether incoming or system-generated (e.g. forms, letters), must receive a unique registration number.-
-Forms are documents, so forms submitted by users must also have metadata as below:.-|
||-Field-||-Description-||
|-*Document Name*-|-Human-readable title-|
|-*Creator / Author*-|-User or system module creating the document-|
|-*Sender / Receiver*-| * -For sent docs: add recipient.-
 * -For received docs: record sender, their reg. number, original date/title.-|
|-*Date*-|-Created and registered timestamps, YYYY-MM-DD-|
|-*Registration Number*-|-MAP automatically assigns a unique document registration number with a prefix and yearly resetting counter (e.g., 2025-IN-0001, 2025-OUT-0002).-|
|-*Original Document Ref.*-|-Links to the original document (e.g. response to request)-|

Enabler includes effort for UI/UX Accessibility Audit activities. | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: By implementing accessibility improvements according to WCAG 2.1 AA and EN 301 549, the Solon Tax product becomes more inclusive and compliant with European accessibility requirements. This ensures equal access for all users, enhances user satisfaction, reduces the risk of non-compliance penalties, and strengthens the product's reputation and market reach in the public sector. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: * Accessibility improvements are implemented according to WCAG 2.1 AA and EN 301 549 standards.

 * Identified accessibility gaps from prior audits or internal reviews are addressed within the scope of the current PI.

 * Key UI components meet minimum color contrast ratios and provide proper focus management.

 * Application is fully navigable via keyboard without loss of functionality.

 * Screen reader users can correctly interpret content structure, labels, and ARIA attributes.

 * QA validation confirms compliance through automated and manual accessibility testing.

 * Documentation is updated to reflect accessibility compliance status and testing results.

IRM: IRM-39738 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: PERFORMANCE EFFICIENCY | Epic: Performance Efficiency Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Reference Data - Implement Enhanced Caching for Reference Data Microservice | Status: Waiting Solution Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 240 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Reference Data - Implement Enhanced Caching for Reference Data Microservice | Enriched Jira Features.Description: We are experiencing severe performance degradation and delays when retrieving reference data. Currently, the system fetches static data from the database for every request, impacting both the UI and BPMN process execution.  The data are mostly static and there is no reason to always fetch it from the DB. 

Requirements: 
 * Implement a caching layer in the Reference data microservice.
 * Eliminate redundant DB queries for static datasets.
 * Cache should persist unless a "data changed" event or manual refresh is triggered.

 

 

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*Documentation*

All configuration options, split strategies, and rule evaluation logic must be fully documented.

Documentation must include (where applicable) :
 * Usage and Configuration examples
 * Reference implementations
 * Operational guidelines , Performance considerations

 

*Non functional requirements*

The solution must maintain or improve the products:

*Performance*  large datasets and multi-sheet evaluation must not degrade processing times
*Security*  no exposure of sensitive configuration data
*Accessibility*  configuration screens and documentation must remain accessible
*Usability*  splitting logic must be understandable and maintainable by admins
Additionally:
The team must collaborate with domain specialists to validate the above.

All Definition of Done ({*}DoD{*}) criteria must be met. | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: Performance issues to be improved. 
Weve identified a significant performance bottleneck in the Reference Data Microservice affecting both UI responsiveness and BPMN throughput. Because this data is largely static, we are proposing the implementation of a caching layer. This will prevent unnecessary database round-trips and provide the high-speed responses required for revenue administration tasks. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: * Implement a caching layer in the Reference data microservice.
 * Eliminate redundant DB queries for static datasets.
 * Cache should persist unless a "data changed" event or manual refresh is triggered.

IRM: IRM-38409 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: USABILITY | Epic: Usability Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: UI/UX Improvements : Interaction friction - View and Edit buttons distiction | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: Other | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 416 | Priority: p2 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: UI/UX Improvements : Interaction friction - View and Edit buttons distiction | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a RM user, I need to be able to clearly distinct if I click to open the record to view or to edit.  

*Background*
In current version, there is no clear distinction between view and edit states. Increase the likelihood of unintended changes.
We need to enable customers to preview records, and if needed perform actions on them.  
To succeed that the record pages should be available in 2 stages : View and Edit. 
Additionally and to be able to streamline the way user reacts with the system:  need to remove double click shortcut in list view items,  and  use click to open a preview drawer. In preview or/and edit pages, the remaining action buttons e.g. status transitions may be available. Additionally in preview page a view the whole record in RO mode and edit/delete buttons should be available. 




*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments. 

 

*Non functional requirements*
It is expected team to get aligned with respective teams and reassure that is not creating issues or the related NFRs will be tested :
Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability 
DODs should be fulfilled. | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: - | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: * Confirm that a single click on a record in a list view opens the "Quick View" summary drawer.
 * Confirm that double-clicking a record in a list view performs no action
 * Confirm that a single click opens the drawer.
 * Confirm that a view menu item is available on list views
 * Confirm that when view item is selected then it opens a drawer displaying record details (Quick view - summary view)
 * Confirm the drawer contains action buttons at the bottom, including an "Edit" button and any applicable status transition buttons (e.g., "Approve," "Reject").
 * Confirm the drawer contains a button/link (e.g., "Open Full View") that navigates the user to the full *read-only* page for that record.
 * Confirm that clicking the "Edit" button within the drawer navigates the user to the full "Edit" mode page for that record. 
 * Confirm that navigating to a record page (either from the drawer's "Full View" button or other links) opens the page in "View" mode by default.
 * Confirm the page title or header clearly indicates "View" mode and that all data fields are presented as non-editable, read-only text.
 * Confirm that attempting to type in fields, change selections in dropdowns, or toggle checkboxes in "View" mode has no effect on the data.
 * Confirm that in "View" mode, an "Edit" button is always displayed, and "Save"/"Cancel" buttons are hidden.
 * Confirm that clicking the "Edit" button (from either the "View" page or the "Quick View" drawer) transitions the page to "Edit" mode.
 * Confirm the page title or header clearly indicates "Edit" mode and that relevant data fields become editable input controls (e.g., text boxes, dropdowns).
 * Confirm that in "Edit" mode, "Save" and "Cancel" buttons are displayed, and the "Edit" button is hidden or disabled
 * Confirm that all primary user actions (View, Edit, Save, Cancel) are initiated via clearly labelled buttons or menu items.
IRM: IRM-38336 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: TRACEABILITY | Epic: Traceability Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Audit Log - Ability to keep Audit trail for code lists /LEFTOVER | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 384 | Priority: p2 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Audit Log - Ability to keep Audit trail for code lists /LEFTOVER | Enriched Jira Features.Description: Leftover from [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-29504] 

In some situations (no parent child relationship) , the audit log entries dont include the information needed to display them in a single, unified list under the parent item or under each related entity.
Example: 
In practice, this means that a codelist can have multiple versions, and each codelist item can also have multiple versions. However, the audit log records for a codelist item are not grouped under one codelist version (or live record). Instead, they are distributed across the various versions, depending on when (version of codelist)  each event was logged.

In scope: 

Codelists

 

*Functional Requirements*
1) I can display all Audit log of the related items under the live record of parent items for the areas: 
 * Reference data (under Codelists)  i.e. Codelists, Codelist items, attributes

2) I can see the history under codelist for all codelist related changes as well as all codelists items related changes. 

 

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments. 

 

*Non functional requirements*
Performance , Security, Accessibility, DODs should be fulfilled.  | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: - | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: 1) I can display all Audit log of  Codelists, Codelist items, attributes

2) I can see in UI the history under codelist for all codelist related changes as well as all codelists items related changes.

IRM: IRM-38242 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: MAINTAINABILITY | Epic: Maintainability Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Improve Dev Experience for local setup | Status: To Do | Requester: Other | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 160 | Priority: p2 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Improve Dev Experience for local setup | Enriched Jira Features.Description: {panel:title=Task}
Increasing the development experience. Eliminate the pain points that developers have while setting up platofrm locally. 
{panel}
{panel:title=Current state}
The biggest problems identified at the time of creating this enabler are:
 * database migration - there is a 99.99% probabilty that the problems occur when running database migration scripts locally. Investigate and intoduce a solution.
 * component tests - it takes forever to rune component tests locally,
 * lack of troubleshooting documentation,
 * slow performance - how can the performance be improved?,
 * local keycloak mostly not working ootb.

Despite above development process forces local testing (which is good). Local tests because of the above issues are very frustrating.
{panel}
{panel:title=Solution}
Find out the root cause of the problems. Come up with solution and implement them. Adjust/create documentation in form of Maintenance Guide O0300.
{panel}
h3. PPD Maturity Index / Control point: Resource Utilization (local resource utilization) / Testability / Technical depth / Development and test environments | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: Increasing Maturity Index. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: * Deliverable -> O0300 Maintenance Guide
IRM: IRM-38230 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: PERFORMANCE EFFICIENCY | Epic: Performance Efficiency Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Green coding Programming Guidelines | Status: To Do | Requester: Other | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 240 | Priority: p2 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Green coding Programming Guidelines | Enriched Jira Features.Description: {panel:title=Task}
To improve the platform maturity index, resource utilization must be optimized. To achieve this, green coding principles should be defined and incorporated into our programming guidelines. The current documentation should be extended to include these rules.
{panel}
{panel:title=Current state}
Currently programming guidelines are described in the following deliverables:

[DD160 - Programming Guidelines|https://goto.netcompany.com/cases/GTE2768/GREPDSOLON/Deliverables/Forms/AllItems.aspx?RootFolder=%2Fcases%2FGTE2768%2FGREPDSOLON%2FDeliverables%2FDD160%20%2D%20Programming%20Guidelines&FolderCTID=0x012000E6A047EE9C5C3B46AF6B4F5F865C09DC&View=%7B1F250723%2DEA5A%2D44A8%2D83D9%2D446989EA7C4A%7D]

[Clean Coding|https://confluence.intrasoft-intl.com/spaces/IC/pages/36142033/Clean+Code]
{panel}
{panel:title=Solution}
Please add green coding rules for the following technologies:
 * Java
 * JavaScript
 * Rego
 * Drools
 * Helm charts
 * Maven
 * PostgreSQL
 * Oracle PL/SQL
 * Liquibase scripts
 * Are docker images used by the platofrm are green friendly? Consider using more greener if possible. Consider create greener docker images -> smaller in size, with dedicated runtimes. IRM-28585 Docker image size optimization

This list should be extended if necessary. These rules should either be integrated into the existing programming guidelines or compiled into a new document dedicated specifically to green coding.
{panel}

IRM: IRM-37871 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: USABILITY | Epic: Usability Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: UI/UX Improvements : Search and navigation : Bars at the top of the pages | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: Other | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 136 | Priority: p2 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: UI/UX Improvements : Search and navigation : Bars at the top of the pages | Enriched Jira Features.Description:  

As a user, I want the main page bar to display only relevant information, include a Save button for quick saving, and show a breadcrumbs bar under the header so that I can easily navigate and manage my work.

 

!image-2026-03-07-23-59-16-316.png! | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: UX Enhancement  ...  | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: Global changes across the app
 * Unnecessary titles (e.g. category) are removed from the main page bar; only relevant information is displayed to user.
 * A Save button is present in the main page bar, allowing users to save changes easily at any time.
 * A breadcrumbs bar is added under the header bar, indicating the user's current location in the application.

As discussed:
 * Data integrity is enforced via optimistic locking (version control).
 * -UI locking is optional and only improves user experience  to reduce user conflicts. The system may implement a soft UI lock when a user enters edit mode.-
 * Conflict handling strategy is required
 * Retry policy for batch/BPMN is required

(Notes 
 * *Optimistic locking* : no long-lived DB lock. Conflict detected when commit

 * *Pessimistic locking* : record locked during editing
) 

*Suggestion*

Each Party record shall include a version attribute, incremented automatically upon every successful update. Before committing any update (UI, batch, workflow, or API), the system shall verify that the submitted version matches the current version stored in the database , or  Reject the transaction if the versions do not match.

The system shall verify that the *submitted version matches the current version* in the database.

{*}Mismatch{*}:
 * The transaction is {*}rejected{*}. A message appears in Ui or an exception if thrown (for the caller)  explaining the concurrency conflict error.
{*}Message{*}: This record was modified by another user. Please reload and review the latest data.

 * UI:  User must reload the record 
 * UI :  User may reapply changes and retry.

 * Batch / BPMN : Retry policy updates  (with a number of attends)
 * Batch / BPMN : Reload latest version? 
 * Batch / BPMN : Log exception

*Release mismatch*
 * The user commits changes

 * The user cancels editing

 * The session times out  or by a configurable defined time out 

*Considerations:* 
Party record may be updated by more than one Forms and a batch process the same time.  (example: A form to update address and meanwhile an older action because of an asynchronous process or a bpmn waiting for an signal to continue to the next step) to update ID was proceeded) 
How long UI lock is valid? Could this version locked may be renewable after a refresh, cancelation, time  etc? 
What happens on browser crash?

IRM: IRM-32912 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: RELIABILITY | Epic: Reliability Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Data Integrity improvements. Error handling in synchronous operations that involve distributed transactions / Registry, Taxpayer | Status: HLD | Requester: Other | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 1600 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Data Integrity improvements. Error handling in synchronous operations that involve distributed transactions / Registry, Taxpayer | Enriched Jira Features.Description: cont.  :https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-25038 

 

Solon Tax microservices have domain boundaries that also encapsulate the corresponding transactional boundaries. I.e. most API operations result in ACID transactions as the updates are handled within the owning microservice's database.

 

However there are some APIs of the system that the owning service also issues PUT/POST requests to different services. For these cases, strong error handling should be introduced.

 

Syncronous operations refer to:
 * HTTP api invocation. A distributed transaction there involves data updates to more than one microservices in the lifecycle of the HTTP request
 * Kafka message consumption. A distributed transaction there involves data updates to more than one microservices in the lifecycle of the kafka message under consuption.

In cases were an operation invokes one or more published messages that are subsequently causing other updates, these are considere eventually consistent transactions and are not in the scope of this enabler.

 

Scope of this enabler is to :

Decide and introduce appropriate error handling for Taxpayer cases as listed in [https://netcompany.sharepoint.com/:x:/s/ICARUSProductTeam/IQDDvVCJsRcQR5si6csRQX4UASFBtrUfVPMWEu6yVXFAQ6w?e=6ZruVa] 
*for " taxpayer", "registration"* 

Consider any patterns to the flows implemented already

Note that the [https://confluence.intrasoft-intl.com/spaces/IC/pages/224722770/Data+integrity+improvements]  

1. Assign worker to a human task.
2. Claim a human task

IRM: IRM-30741 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: MAINTAINABILITY | Epic: Maintainability Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Introduce ArchUnit | Status: HLD | Requester: Other | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 400 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Introduce ArchUnit | Enriched Jira Features.Description: *Problem Statement*

As the SolonTax codebase grows in size and complexity, it becomes increasingly difficult to manually enforce architectural guidelines and design principles ( see D0160 Programming Guidelines) during code reviews. This leads to several risks:
 * *Architectural Drift:* Over time, the code can deviate from its intended design (e.g., layered architecture, domain model purity), leading to tight coupling and reduced maintainability.
 * *Inconsistent Code Reviews:* Architectural violations can be easily missed during manual reviews, as reviewers are often focused on business logic.
 * *Increased Technical Debt:* Unchecked violations accumulate as technical debt, making future development, refactoring, and onboarding of new team members more difficult and costly.

There is currently no automated mechanism to prevent such architectural decay, making the system's long-term health dependent on tribal knowledge and manual vigilance.

*Proposed Solution*

This enabler will introduce {*}ArchUnit{*}, a free Java library for checking the architecture of your code, into our build and test lifecycle. By writing plain Java unit tests, we can codify our architectural rules and automatically verify them.

The solution involves:
 # *Integrating ArchUnit:* Add the ArchUnit dependency to the project's build configuration (e.g., Maven or Gradle).
 # *Creating an Architecture Test Suite:* Establish a dedicated test source set or package for architectural tests.
 # *Implementing Foundational Rules:* Implement an initial set of high-value architectural rules to serve as a baseline and a template for future rules. These tests will run as part of the standard CI/CD pipeline, failing the build if a violation is detected.

This will provide immediate, automated feedback to developers and act as a powerful "guardrail" to prevent architectural erosion.

*Acceptance Criteria*
 # *Dependency Integration:* The ArchUnit library is successfully added as a test-scoped dependency.
 # *Test Suite Creation:* A dedicated maven module is created to house all ArchUnit tests.
 # *CI/CD Integration:* The architectural test suite is configured to run automatically as part of the continuous integration pipeline during unit tests phase. A build must fail if any architectural rule is violated.
 # *Baseline Pass:* All newly introduced architectural tests pass against the existing codebase on the main development branch. If any pre-existing violations are found, they must be either fixed or explicitly exempted as part of this task's scope.

*Out of Scope*
 * This enabler focuses on establishing the framework and implementing a foundational set of rules. Defining an exhaustive list of every possible architectural rule is not in scope.
 * Large-scale refactoring of the existing codebase to fix numerous pre-existing violations is out of scope, unless a small, agreed-upon number of fixes are required to establish a clean baseline. | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: - | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: As per description

IRM: IRM-20329 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: SECURITY | Epic: Security Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Data Security - Restrict Access to Personal Data GDPR- Admin (based on data classifications) - Part 1/4 | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: Other | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 1304 | Priority: p2 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Data Security - Restrict Access to Personal Data GDPR- Admin (based on data classifications) - Part 1/4 | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As an admin, I want to restrict access to sensitive personal data, so that only users that have a legitimate reason to access this data are granted access and unauthorized access to this data is prevented.

*Introduction*

This feature is related to the epic IRM-3106 in which requirements have been documented to secure the information in the revenue management system from unauthorized access.

This feature is related to IRM-30322 in which requirements have been documented to classify fields  (or characteristics or categories of attachments) in the application as fields that contain non-personal, personal or sensitive personal data GDPR. However, not each field that has been classified to contain (sensitive) personal data will always contain personal data, as these fields (e.g. identifier or address fields) may also be used to record data for parties that are not natural persons. Only if the data in these fields is related to a natural person (see IRM-20315), it can be considered personal data. Exception to this rule is data that cannot be related to or has not yet been related to a specific party, such as data in forms, uploaded payment data or messages in the message store that cannot or not yet be related to a specific party. This data should be considered personal if the data has been classified as such.
Depends on [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-20322] 

 

*Out of scope :* 
Archive db
Define classifications for financial details and relevant datasets (see [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-23836] )

 

+Clarifications:+
classify fields  : as discussed  we mean restrict access to records based on record type and defined classification levels 

+Expected Behaviors to be available :+ 
+Visibility:+ 
Field masking, e.g. Name = *****
Record hidden , e.g. record not returned
+Search+
Record hidden, e.g., No results returned, Result excluded completely
Field masking,  e.g., Result returned but masked
+Logs+
Logs should be immutable. Information may be masked. 
 

*Functional Requirements*

*For Party , Party Roles, Attachments:*  
 * Admin can restrict access to sensitive personal data based on classification level and group of users (e.g. using user access groups).
The classification levels are defined in  [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-20322] 

 * Admin can restrict based on classification levels, who can :
 ** _Create_
 ** _Read ( 2 modes to be able to be configured :  masked or not listing the record)_ 
 ** _Update_  
 ** _Delete_
 ** _Search_ 
 ** The above permissions must be enforceable for operations initiated via the UI, direct service calls, or APIs.
_Suggestion:  Data Access Layer Enforcement of permissions_
 **  __ It is expected that the visibility of the classified details may be configured by configurators as : masked or non visible. (see also ILs)

 * Admin should be able to remove (masking or removing record visibility)  access of records based on classification levels, from data areas of Party,  party role, Attachments

+Examples:+ 
An Admin can successfully configure a User Access Group to have "Read" access to "Personal Data" but be denied "Read" access to "Sensitive Personal Data".
When a user from that group views a list of parties, parties with only "Personal Data" are visible, while parties with "Sensitive Personal Data" are either hidden or have their sensitive fields masked, as configured.
When the same user performs a search, the results correctly exclude or mask records containing "Sensitive Personal Data".

*{color:#172b4d}Identification Labels{color}*
 * {color:#172b4d}Identification labels should be displayed according the relevant classifications restrictions. 
E.g. : If the identifier used in IL (i.e. the primary) is sensitive and not visible by user  (John Takis, Tax Identification Number: 123456789) 
a) if the mode is to mask sensitive detail -> IL appears with stars instead of identifier. (John Takis, Tax Identification Number: ********** )
b) if the mode is that the data should not appear in the results -> IL appears  with empty details  (John Takis, Tax Identification Number:  ){color}{color:#172b4d}Similarly in other ILs related with classified data. {color}

{color:#172b4d}*Message store*{color}
 * {color:#172b4d}Admin should be able to remove (masking or removing record visibility)  access of records based on classification levels, from Message store. Permission set as per above mentioned list (view, search ,etc.).{color}

*{color:#172b4d}Operational Reports{color}*
 * {color:#172b4d}Visibility of records in Operational reports are restricted (masking or removing record visibility) based on above mentioned classification levels and permissions. {color}

*{color:#172b4d}Other related entities/cross-entity propagation{color}*
 * {color:#172b4d}Restrictions must propagate to any entity that displays or uses classified data.
Visibility of records in all system records*  are restricted (masking or removing record visibility) based on above mentioned classification levels and permissions.
*Examples :  {color}

 * 
 ** Forms,
 ** Cases,
 ** Human task,
 ** Taxpayer accounts related (e.g. : liabilities, bill segments, bills, Fts, Journal entries, suppression, assessments)
 ** Registration related (e.g. : Candidate lists, Operational Plans, Calendar records - timeoff, assignments-, Organizational units , Asset relationships,  revenue type Registrations, Obligations, user right) 
 ** Users, user roles,  Object access groups
 ** Notifications
 ** Contacts
 ** Notes

 

*Governance* 
The permissions will be defined by admin as described In [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-39113] 

 

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments. 

 

*Non functional requirements*
It is expected to reassure that relevant NFRs (Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability ) are tested and are not negatively affecting the product.  
DODs should be fulfilled.

Notes: 

!image-2025-06-17-07-42-29-150.png|width=761,height=434! | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: Enabling administrators to restrict access to sensitive personal data based on defined classifications will significantly strengthen data privacy, compliance, and governance within Solon Tax. By allowing granular control over who can read, update, or delete personal dataeither via the UI or APIsorganizations can enforce data protection policies aligned with legal and regulatory requirements (e.g., GDPR). The ability to configure whether restricted information is masked, encrypted, or hidden entirely enhances both transparency and control. Additionally, extending data privacy protections to logs, messages, and other data sources ensures that sensitive details are not inadvertently exposed, even during exception handling or auditing. This functionality will reduce the risk of unauthorized data access, support compliance, and build greater trust with end users and stakeholders. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: *A) For Party , Party Roles, Attachments:*

IRM: IRM-38336 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: TRACEABILITY | Epic: Traceability Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Audit Log - Ability to keep Audit trail for code lists /LEFTOVER | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 384 | Priority: p2 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Audit Log - Ability to keep Audit trail for code lists /LEFTOVER | Enriched Jira Features.Description: Leftover from [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-29504] 

In some situations (no parent child relationship) , the audit log entries don’t include the information needed to display them in a single, unified list under the parent item or under each related entity.
Example: 
In practice, this means that a codelist can have multiple versions, and each codelist item can also have multiple versions. However, the audit log records for a codelist item are not grouped under one codelist version (or live record). Instead, they are distributed across the various versions, depending on when (version of codelist)  each event was logged.

IRM: IRM-36862 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: RELIABILITY | Epic: Reliability Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Record Locking - Apply logic to  Party record | Status: HLD | Requester: GRC | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 1600 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Record Locking - Apply logic to  Party record | Enriched Jira Features.Description: The system manages simultaneous record modifications through a  mechanism, ensuring consistent updates and providing users with confirmation on whether their commit was accepted.

As discussed:
 * Data integrity is enforced via optimistic locking (version control).
 * -UI locking is optional and only improves user experience  to reduce user conflicts. The system may implement a soft UI lock when a user enters edit mode.-
 * Conflict handling strategy is required
 * Retry policy for batch/BPMN is required

(Notes 
 * *Optimistic locking* : no long-lived DB lock. Conflict detected when commit

 * *Pessimistic locking* : record locked during editing
) 

*Suggestion*

Each Party record shall include a version attribute, incremented automatically upon every successful update. Before committing any update (UI, batch, workflow, or API), the system shall verify that the submitted version matches the current version stored in the database , or  Reject the transaction if the versions do not match.

The system shall verify that the *submitted version matches the current version* in the database.

{*}Mismatch{*}:
 * The transaction is {*}rejected{*}. A message appears in Ui or an exception if thrown (for the caller)  explaining the concurrency conflict error.
{*}Message{*}: “This record was modified by another user. Please reload and review the latest data.”

 * UI:  User must reload the record 
 * UI :  User may reapply changes and retry.

 * Batch / BPMN : Retry policy updates  (with a number of attends)
 * Batch / BPMN : Reload latest version? 
 * Batch / BPMN : Log exception

*Release mismatch*
 * The user commits changes

 * The user cancels editing

 * The session times out  or by a configurable defined time out 

*Considerations:* 
Party record may be updated by more than one Forms and a batch process the same time.  (example: A form to update address and meanwhile an older action because of an asynchronous process or a bpmn waiting for an signal to continue to the next step) to update ID was proceeded) 
How long UI lock is valid? Could this version locked may be renewable after a refresh, cancelation, time  etc? 
What happens on browser crash?

IRM: IRM-32912 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: RELIABILITY | Epic: Reliability Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Data Integrity improvements. Error handling in synchronous operations that involve distributed transactions / Registry, Taxpayer | Status: HLD | Requester: Other | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 1600 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Data Integrity improvements. Error handling in synchronous operations that involve distributed transactions / Registry, Taxpayer | Enriched Jira Features.Description: cont.  :https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-25038 

 

Solon Tax microservices have domain boundaries that also encapsulate the corresponding transactional boundaries. I.e. most API operations result in ACID transactions as the updates are handled within the owning microservice's database.

 

However there are some APIs of the system that the owning service also issues PUT/POST requests to different services. For these cases, strong error handling should be introduced.

 

Syncronous operations refer to:
 * HTTP api invocation. A distributed transaction there involves data updates to more than one microservices in the lifecycle of the HTTP request
 * Kafka message consumption. A distributed transaction there involves data updates to more than one microservices in the lifecycle of the kafka message under consuption.

In cases were an operation invokes one or more published messages that are subsequently causing other updates, these are considere eventually consistent transactions and are not in the scope of this enabler.

 

Scope of this enabler is to :

Decide and introduce appropriate error handling for Taxpayer cases as listed in [https://netcompany.sharepoint.com/:x:/s/ICARUSProductTeam/IQDDvVCJsRcQR5si6csRQX4UASFBtrUfVPMWEu6yVXFAQ6w?e=6ZruVa] 
*for " taxpayer", "registration"* 

Consider any patterns to the flows implemented already

Note that the [https://confluence.intrasoft-intl.com/spaces/IC/pages/224722770/Data+integrity+improvements]  

1. Assign worker to a human task.
2. Claim a human task

IRM: IRM-30741 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: MAINTAINABILITY | Epic: Maintainability Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Introduce ArchUnit | Status: HLD | Requester: Other | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 400 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Introduce ArchUnit | Enriched Jira Features.Description: *Problem Statement*

As the SolonTax codebase grows in size and complexity, it becomes increasingly difficult to manually enforce architectural guidelines and design principles ( see D0160 Programming Guidelines) during code reviews. This leads to several risks:
 * *Architectural Drift:* Over time, the code can deviate from its intended design (e.g., layered architecture, domain model purity), leading to tight coupling and reduced maintainability.
 * *Inconsistent Code Reviews:* Architectural violations can be easily missed during manual reviews, as reviewers are often focused on business logic.
 * *Increased Technical Debt:* Unchecked violations accumulate as technical debt, making future development, refactoring, and onboarding of new team members more difficult and costly.

There is currently no automated mechanism to prevent such architectural decay, making the system's long-term health dependent on tribal knowledge and manual vigilance.

*Proposed Solution*

This enabler will introduce {*}ArchUnit{*}, a free Java library for checking the architecture of your code, into our build and test lifecycle. By writing plain Java unit tests, we can codify our architectural rules and automatically verify them.

The solution involves:
 # *Integrating ArchUnit:* Add the ArchUnit dependency to the project's build configuration (e.g., Maven or Gradle).
 # *Creating an Architecture Test Suite:* Establish a dedicated test source set or package for architectural tests.
 # *Implementing Foundational Rules:* Implement an initial set of high-value architectural rules to serve as a baseline and a template for future rules. These tests will run as part of the standard CI/CD pipeline, failing the build if a violation is detected.

This will provide immediate, automated feedback to developers and act as a powerful "guardrail" to prevent architectural erosion.

*Acceptance Criteria*
 # *Dependency Integration:* The ArchUnit library is successfully added as a test-scoped dependency.
 # *Test Suite Creation:* A dedicated maven module is created to house all ArchUnit tests.
 # *CI/CD Integration:* The architectural test suite is configured to run automatically as part of the continuous integration pipeline during unit tests phase. A build must fail if any architectural rule is violated.
 # *Baseline Pass:* All newly introduced architectural tests pass against the existing codebase on the main development branch. If any pre-existing violations are found, they must be either fixed or explicitly exempted as part of this task's scope.

*Out of Scope*
 * This enabler focuses on establishing the framework and implementing a foundational set of rules. Defining an exhaustive list of every possible architectural rule is not in scope.
 * Large-scale refactoring of the existing codebase to fix numerous pre-existing violations is out of scope, unless a small, agreed-upon number of fixes are required to establish a clean baseline. | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: - | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: As per description

{color:#0747a6}*BECAUSE OF THE COMPAXITY OF THE TOOL TO BE IMPLEMENTED WE WILL INITIATE THE DESIGN BY A POC.* {color}

Configuration Data
 * Entity types (c_ objects) , Codelists/codelist items, , System parameters (codelist item attributes), 
queries, other config data (users, exchange rates, calendars, worker profiles, roles, object access groups, user access groups, ledgers, GL accounts numbers, rates etc), UI schemas/forms.'

Translations
 * Labels ( _l objects) 

TBC: 
 * (?) User defined characteristics,
 * Drools
 * (?) Other customizations

Ownerships 
 * Config items are flagged with its ownership , i.e. :  on who is responsible for their maintenance (Product team, national delivery team, or client-specific team) restricting areas that should not be used,  their intended scope of usage / applicability (global, regional, or specific clients) , whether they are reusable across implementations Additionally provide controlling mechanism on which items based on owner are eligible to be migrated (e.g. do not deploy base items, unless it is an attribute of a system parameter, entity schema help url, or labels.)   [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-26335]  

*Functional Requirements:*

*+Preparation+* 
 * *Prerequisites*
 ** Define environments that can be source and destinations
 ** Define the versioning numbering that will be used for all the items (?)
 * *Flag configuration items*
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin should label Ownership of the component. 
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin may label configurations implemented as  "Ready for export".  ([https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/PSD-11032)|https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/PSD-11032])
 ** Beforehand, version of the items to be migrated may be defined. 
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin optionally may label the component with the Functionality or Scope or Product component will support.  
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin may select if the Cong items will be activated while migrated or will remain inactive till admin manually activate them the destination environment. 
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin may upload the file where applicable (labels - translations) should be uploaded. 
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin may select the source and destination environments.  

 * *Roles and permissions*
 ** Permitted users can use the packaging tool and perform the mentioned actions

              consideration :  ? Could it be extended to use approval processes?

 

*+Core+*
 * *Ui*
 ** Admin may see the details of previous local releases/ deployments as well as historical data on the local releases/ deployments
 ** Admin/developer may check out and then check in any non Base config item
 *** Checked in item receives automatically a version
 *** Validation when trying to check out a Base item
 ** Admin may initiate a new deployment (create release) 
 *** Select source and destination environment
 *** UI or CLI to *select/export/inspect/import* configurations, code, flows, templates, etc.
 *** Select to proceed with the deployment
 *** Admin may use filters  (as per flags added above , version number ,  along with other items e.g. category field) to locate the items to be included in the package. 
 *** Admin can add comments per item and per local release. 
 ** Admin may see details under each logged release
 *** Admin can see timestamp and historical details on the local release. 
 *** Admin can see list of exceptions before and after the deployment
 ** Admin after deployment will be able to make effective/enable the version/selected items in destination environment. 

 

+*Deployment process*+

 
 * *Suggest items to be selected*
 ** Provide Delta support to select elements that are new or modified -  where applicable.
 ** Exclude BASE items with exceptions (help urls, labels, attributes in system parameters).
 ** Indicate possible conflicts.
 * *Dependency management*  - Select items to be migrated (metadata, content ... ) from a list .
 ** Identify dependencies and indicate what related items need to move together.
Identify and warn if related components must be exported together.
 ** Support  when certain settings (like endpoint URLs, external credentials, currency precision) may need to differ by environment - need a way to parameterize or externalize environment-specific config.)

 * *Standard Format & Packaging*
 ** Define a standard export/import format   (e.g., JSON, XML, YAML or other per component type) 
 ** Group exported artifacts into packages. 
 ** Be able to define the expiration date / inactivation date of an older version per component and have available mechanisms to validate that the new version will be available when old is expired. 
 *  *Import & Validation* : 
 ** Examine if needs to define states for each deployable (e.g., {_}Draft → Approved → Deployed → Deprecated{_}).
 ** Ensure compatibility and prevent unintended overwrites.
 ** Run automated validations in a dry run mode
 ** Indicate possible conflicts.
 ** Simulate a deployment before actual promotion
 ** Advice smoke testing after deployment

 * *Auditability and Reporting* 
 ** Audit Trail of  who changed what, when, and where in the target environment. (See also relevant section on  [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-27058] ) 
 ** Be able to see the result of the migration process. Monitor what succeeded, failed, or was skipped.
 
 * *Rollback Mechanism  / go back to a previous version*  
 ** Ability to revert a deployment if needed either fully or selectively.  See also relevant section on  [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-27058] 
 ** Ability to set when old version should be expired as new version should be active.  See also relevant section on  [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-27058] 

 * Compliance/ *Data security* privacy (Certain configuration or integration artifacts may handle sensitive data)
 ** Dev and Stg environments are created without taxpayer data, but include configuration and custom logic. i.e.,  when exporting from production to other envs, do not deploy data. 
 * Other
 ** Consider also translation management needs as described in  IRM-24809  

 

 

*Documentation*
 * Documentation will be delivered with the steps to install the application and tools needed plus how to use the tool with example. 

*Non Functional Requirements:*
 * Tool can be handled by delivery teams.
 * Performance and security DODs should be considered.
