IRM: IRM-20329 | Initiative Group: NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | Initiative: SECURITY | Epic: Security Enhancements | Roadmap Feature: Data Security - Restrict Access to Personal Data GDPR- Admin (based on data classifications) - Part 1/4 | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: Other | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 1304 | Priority: p2 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: Data Security - Restrict Access to Personal Data GDPR- Admin (based on data classifications) - Part 1/4 | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As an admin, I want to restrict access to sensitive personal data, so that only users that have a legitimate reason to access this data are granted access and unauthorized access to this data is prevented.

*Introduction*

This feature is related to the epic IRM-3106 in which requirements have been documented to secure the information in the revenue management system from unauthorized access.

This feature is related to IRM-30322 in which requirements have been documented to classify fields  (or characteristics or categories of attachments) in the application as fields that contain non-personal, personal or sensitive personal data GDPR. However, not each field that has been classified to contain (sensitive) personal data will always contain personal data, as these fields (e.g. identifier or address fields) may also be used to record data for parties that are not natural persons. Only if the data in these fields is related to a natural person (see IRM-20315), it can be considered personal data. Exception to this rule is data that cannot be related to or has not yet been related to a specific party, such as data in forms, uploaded payment data or messages in the message store that cannot or not yet be related to a specific party. This data should be considered personal if the data has been classified as such.
Depends on [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-20322] 

 

*Out of scope :* 
Archive db
Define classifications for financial details and relevant datasets (see [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-23836] )

 

+Clarifications:+
classify fields  : as discussed  we mean restrict access to records based on record type and defined classification levels 

+Expected Behaviors to be available :+ 
+Visibility:+ 
Field masking, e.g. Name = *****
Record hidden , e.g. record not returned
+Search+
Record hidden, e.g., No results returned, Result excluded completely
Field masking,  e.g., Result returned but masked
+Logs+
Logs should be immutable. Information may be masked. 
 

*Functional Requirements*

*For Party , Party Roles, Attachments:*  
 * Admin can restrict access to sensitive personal data based on classification level and group of users (e.g. using user access groups).
The classification levels are defined in  [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-20322] 

 * Admin can restrict based on classification levels, who can :
 ** _Create_
 ** _Read ( 2 modes to be able to be configured :  masked or not listing the record)_ 
 ** _Update_  
 ** _Delete_
 ** _Search_ 
 ** The above permissions must be enforceable for operations initiated via the UI, direct service calls, or APIs.
_Suggestion:  Data Access Layer Enforcement of permissions_
 **  __ It is expected that the visibility of the classified details may be configured by configurators as : masked or non visible. (see also ILs)

 * Admin should be able to remove (masking or removing record visibility)  access of records based on classification levels, from data areas of Party,  party role, Attachments

+Examples:+ 
An Admin can successfully configure a User Access Group to have "Read" access to "Personal Data" but be denied "Read" access to "Sensitive Personal Data".
When a user from that group views a list of parties, parties with only "Personal Data" are visible, while parties with "Sensitive Personal Data" are either hidden or have their sensitive fields masked, as configured.
When the same user performs a search, the results correctly exclude or mask records containing "Sensitive Personal Data".

*{color:#172b4d}Identification Labels{color}*
 * {color:#172b4d}Identification labels should be displayed according the relevant classifications restrictions. 
E.g. : If the identifier used in IL (i.e. the primary) is sensitive and not visible by user  (John Takis, Tax Identification Number: 123456789) 
a) if the mode is to mask sensitive detail -> IL appears with stars instead of identifier. (John Takis, Tax Identification Number: ********** )
b) if the mode is that the data should not appear in the results -> IL appears  with empty details  (John Takis, Tax Identification Number:  ){color}{color:#172b4d}Similarly in other ILs related with classified data. {color}

{color:#172b4d}*Message store*{color}
 * {color:#172b4d}Admin should be able to remove (masking or removing record visibility)  access of records based on classification levels, from Message store. Permission set as per above mentioned list (view, search ,etc.).{color}

*{color:#172b4d}Operational Reports{color}*
 * {color:#172b4d}Visibility of records in Operational reports are restricted (masking or removing record visibility) based on above mentioned classification levels and permissions. {color}

*{color:#172b4d}Other related entities/cross-entity propagation{color}*
 * {color:#172b4d}Restrictions must propagate to any entity that displays or uses classified data.
Visibility of records in all system records*  are restricted (masking or removing record visibility) based on above mentioned classification levels and permissions.
*Examples :  {color}

 * 
 ** Forms,
 ** Cases,
 ** Human task,
 ** Taxpayer accounts related (e.g. : liabilities, bill segments, bills, Fts, Journal entries, suppression, assessments)
 ** Registration related (e.g. : Candidate lists, Operational Plans, Calendar records - timeoff, assignments-, Organizational units , Asset relationships,  revenue type Registrations, Obligations, user right) 
 ** Users, user roles,  Object access groups
 ** Notifications
 ** Contacts
 ** Notes

 

*Governance* 
The permissions will be defined by admin as described In [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-39113] 

 

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments. 

 

*Non functional requirements*
It is expected to reassure that relevant NFRs (Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability ) are tested and are not negatively affecting the product.  
DODs should be fulfilled.

!image-2025-06-17-07-42-29-150.png|width=761,height=434! | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: Enabling administrators to restrict access to sensitive personal data based on defined classifications will significantly strengthen data privacy, compliance, and governance within Solon Tax. By allowing granular control over who can read, update, or delete personal data—either via the UI or APIs—organizations can enforce data protection policies aligned with legal and regulatory requirements (e.g., GDPR). The ability to configure whether restricted information is masked, encrypted, or hidden entirely enhances both transparency and control. Additionally, extending data privacy protections to logs, messages, and other data sources ensures that sensitive details are not inadvertently exposed, even during exception handling or auditing. This functionality will reduce the risk of unauthorized data access, support compliance, and build greater trust with end users and stakeholders. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: *A) For Party , Party Roles, Attachments:*

IRM: IRM-38759 | Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Initiative: VAT | Epic: Reference Implemenation - VAT | Roadmap Feature: VAT Tax Account Reference Implementation | Status: HLD | Requester: GTM | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 159 | Priority: p1 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: VAT Tax Account Reference Implementation | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a revenue officer, I would like to add debts and payments to a tax account, so that I am able to demo how Solon supports a VAT account (i.e., Tax Account only for VAT).

*Introduction* 

This feature aims to create the necessary configuration for a Tax Account reference imp[lementation. The Overview of the Tax Account that is needed in all implementations using a Tax Account is in scope of feature ... 

*Functional Requirements*

*Core Configuration Requirements*
 # *Revenue Type Configuration*

 * *"VAT for Tax Account" Revenue Type* with flags:
 * taxAccount: true - Enable tax account functionality
 * reconciliationPeriod: true - Enable reconciliation period support

 * {*}Revenue Type Category{*}: PERIODIC
 * {*}Revenue Type Actions{*}: FILING, PAYMENT
 * {*}Calendar Integration{*}: Link to appropriate revenue calendars{*}{{*}}

 
 * *"VAT for Tax Account Ad hoc" Revenue Type* with flags:

 * 
 ** taxAccount: true - Enable tax account functionality
 ** reconciliationPeriod: true - Enable reconciliation period support

 * {*}Revenue Type Category{*}: Ad Hoc
 * {*}Revenue Type Actions{*}: PAYMENT

 
 # *Reconciliation Period Management*

 * *Reconciliation Period Entity* configuration with:
 * Period codes (e.g., "2024M1", "2024M2")
 * Start and end dates for each period
 * Active/Inactive status management

 * *Revenue Type Registration Reconciliation Period* linking:
 * Opening and closing balances per period
 * Party informed indicator

 # *Financial Transaction-Reconciliation period*

 * {*}FT Reconciliation Period Link{*}: Enable FTs to reference reconciliation periods
 * {*}Automatic Period Assignment{*}: Link FTs to reconciliation periods based on creation date
 * {*}Validation Rules{*}: Ensure only revenue types with reconciliationPeriod: true can link to periods

 # *Tax Account UI Configuration*

 * {*}Specialized UI Schema{*}: entitySubType: 'TaxAcc_RP' for Revenue Type Registration
 * {*}Balance Display{*}: Show opening/closing balances per reconciliation period
 * {*}Period Timeline{*}: Visual representation of reconciliation periods
 * {*}Balance Update Interface{*}: Enable manual balance adjustments with audit trail

*Business Process Requirements*
 # *Balance Management*

 * {*}Opening Balance Recording{*}: Support initial balance entry per reconciliation period
 * {*}Closing Balance Calculation{*}: Automatic calculation based on transactions and adjustments
 * {*}Balance Transfer{*}: Opening balance of next period equals closing balance of previous period
 * {*}Manual Adjustments{*}: Allow authorized balance corrections with proper validation

 # *Debt and Payment Processing*

 * {*}Debt Recording{*}: Create financial transactions for VAT liabilities
 * {*}Payment Processing{*}: Record and allocate VAT payments to specific periods
 * {*}Cross-Period Allocation{*}: Support payment allocation across multiple reconciliation periods
 * {*}Interest and Penalty Calculation{*}: Apply to overdue amounts per period

 

*Documentation*
Document all the above configuration for introducing a reference implementation for the Tax Account is vital for Demos and future implementation needs. 

 

  | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: By enhancing Solon Tax with a reference implementation for VAT Tax Account functionality, we will enable revenue officers to efficiently manage VAT debts and payments through reconciliation periods, providing a comprehensive demonstration of Solon Tax's capability to support requirements for VAT Tax Account. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria:  Revenue Type VAT is configured with both taxAccount and reconciliationPeriod flags enabled
 Reconciliation periods can be created, updated, and linked to VAT revenue type registrations
 Financial transactions automatically link to appropriate reconciliation periods based on creation date
 Opening and closing balances can be recorded and maintained per reconciliation period
 Tax Account UI displays comprehensive period timeline with balance information
 Revenue officers can add debts (assessments) and record payments against specific reconciliation periods
 Balance calculations are accurate across period boundaries
 Party informed status can be tracked and updated per reconciliation period
 System validates that only reconciliation-period-enabled revenue types support period functionality
 Audit trail captures all balance changes and period-related activities

Documentation on the configuration guide for the necessary configuration needed to have the reference implementation of the Tax Account up and running. 
IRM: IRM-38710 | Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Initiative: VAT | Epic: Reference Implemenation - VAT | Roadmap Feature: VAT Return Form - Warning for Intracommunity Transaction Enhancement | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GTM | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 80 | Priority: p2 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: VAT Return Form - Warning for Intracommunity Transaction Enhancement | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a RM User, I would like to see a warning when I fill in intracommunity transaction fields in the VAT Return Form, so that I am informed of my obligations to submit the corresponding VIES Statement in the respective deadline.

*Introduction* 

This feature enhances the VAT Return Form by implementing a warning mechanism for intracommunity transactions. The enhancement includes field label corrections to enhance understanding of these fields and a business-critical warning to ensure taxpayers comply with VIES Statement submission requirements. 

 

*Functional Requirements*

*Field Label Corrections*
The following field labels in the VAT Return Form will be renamed to accurately reflect their purpose:

VAT on Sales Section:

TOTAL SALES BUYER OBLIGATED ? Intracommunity Sales
TOTAL SALES BUYER NOT OBLIGATED ? Intracommunity Sales without VAT
VAT on Purchases Section:

TOTAL PURCHASES BUYER OBLIGED FOR VAT ? Intracommunity Purchases
TOTAL PURCHASES BUYER NOT OBLIGED FOR VAT ? Intracommunity Purchases without VAT



*Warning Implementation*
When any of the intracommunity transaction fields contain values, the system shall display a warning message:

Warning Message:

"For these transactions, in addition to the VAT return, you are required to submit the corresponding *VIES Statement* by the 25th day of the following month."

Warning Behavior:
 * Warning appears when any intracommunity field has a non-zero value
 * User can proceed with form submission despite the warning
 * Warning persists until form is submitted or fields are cleared | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: This enhancement aims to showcase an example of Solon Tax capability for warnings. Business case aims to reduce taxpayer compliance errors by providing clear field labeling and proactive warnings about VIES Statement obligations. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: h3. Field Label Updates

All four intracommunity transaction fields display updated labels as specified below: 

VAT on Sales Section:

{{TOTAL SALES BUYER OBLIGATED}} ? *{{Intracommunity Sales}}*

{{TOTAL SALES BUYER NOT OBLIGATED}} ? *{{Intracommunity Sales without VAT}}*
VAT on Purchases Section:

{{TOTAL PURCHASES BUYER OBLIGED FOR VAT}} ? *{{Intracommunity Purchases}}*

{{TOTAL PURCHASES BUYER NOT OBLIGED FOR VAT}} ? *{{Intracommunity Purchases without VAT}}*
 * Labels are consistent across all form views (edit, read-only, validation)
 * Field functionality remains unchanged - only labels are updated

h3. Warning Implementation

When any of the intracommunity transaction fields contain values, the system shall display a warning message:

*Warning Message:*
{quote}"For these transactions, in addition to the VAT return, you are required to submit the corresponding *VIES Statement* by the 25th day of the following month."
{quote}
h3. Warning Display Logic
 * Warning appears when any intracommunity field (Amount or Adjustment) contains non-zero values
 * Warning message displays the exact text specified above with "{*}VIES Statement{*}" in bold
 * Warning is classified as a warning (not error) allowing form submission to proceed
 * No impact on existing form functionality or performance

h3. Warning Persistence
 * Warning remains visible throughout form editing session
 * Warning disappears when all intracommunity fields are cleared/set to zero
 * Warning does not prevent form validation, saving, or submission

h3. User Experience
 * Warning appears in the standard warning notification area
 * Warning uses appropriate warning styling (amber/yellow color scheme)
 * Warning includes appropriate warning icon
 * Warning message is clearly readable and professionally formatted

• Opening and closing balances can be recorded and maintained per reconciliation period
• Tax Account UI displays comprehensive period timeline with balance information
• Revenue officers can add debts (assessments) and record payments against specific reconciliation periods
• Balance calculations are accurate across period boundaries
• Party informed status can be tracked and updated per reconciliation period
• System validates that only reconciliation-period-enabled revenue types support period functionality
• Audit trail captures all balance changes and period-related activities

Documentation on the configuration guide for the necessary configuration needed to have the reference implementation of the Tax Account up and running. 
IRM: IRM-38710 | Initiative Group: REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | Initiative: VAT | Epic: Reference Implemenation - VAT | Roadmap Feature: VAT Return Form - Warning for Intracommunity Transaction Enhancement | Status: Waiting Analysis Approval | Requester: GTM | Calculated PI: PI28 | Final Original Estimate: 80 | Priority: p2 | Enriched Jira Features.Summary: VAT Return Form - Warning for Intracommunity Transaction Enhancement | Enriched Jira Features.Description: As a RM User, I would like to see a warning when I fill in intracommunity transaction fields in the VAT Return Form, so that I am informed of my obligations to submit the corresponding VIES Statement in the respective deadline.

*Introduction* 

This feature enhances the VAT Return Form by implementing a warning mechanism for intracommunity transactions. The enhancement includes field label corrections to enhance understanding of these fields and a business-critical warning to ensure taxpayers comply with VIES Statement submission requirements. 

 

*Functional Requirements*

*Field Label Corrections*
The following field labels in the VAT Return Form will be renamed to accurately reflect their purpose:

VAT on Sales Section:

TOTAL SALES BUYER OBLIGATED → Intracommunity Sales
TOTAL SALES BUYER NOT OBLIGATED → Intracommunity Sales without VAT
VAT on Purchases Section:

TOTAL PURCHASES BUYER OBLIGED FOR VAT → Intracommunity Purchases
TOTAL PURCHASES BUYER NOT OBLIGED FOR VAT → Intracommunity Purchases without VAT



*Warning Implementation*
When any of the intracommunity transaction fields contain values, the system shall display a warning message:

Warning Message:

"For these transactions, in addition to the VAT return, you are required to submit the corresponding *VIES Statement* by the 25th day of the following month."

Warning Behavior:
 * Warning appears when any intracommunity field has a non-zero value
 * User can proceed with form submission despite the warning
 * Warning persists until form is submitted or fields are cleared | Enriched Jira Features.Benefit Hypothesis: This enhancement aims to showcase an example of Solon Tax capability for warnings. Business case aims to reduce taxpayer compliance errors by providing clear field labeling and proactive warnings about VIES Statement obligations. | Enriched Jira Features.Acceptance Criteria: h3. Field Label Updates

All four intracommunity transaction fields display updated labels as specified below: 

VAT on Sales Section:

{{TOTAL SALES BUYER OBLIGATED}} → *{{Intracommunity Sales}}*

{{TOTAL SALES BUYER NOT OBLIGATED}} → *{{Intracommunity Sales without VAT}}*
VAT on Purchases Section:

{{TOTAL PURCHASES BUYER OBLIGED FOR VAT}} → *{{Intracommunity Purchases}}*

{{TOTAL PURCHASES BUYER NOT OBLIGED FOR VAT}} → *{{Intracommunity Purchases without VAT}}*
 * Labels are consistent across all form views (edit, read-only, validation)
 * Field functionality remains unchanged - only labels are updated

h3. Warning Implementation

When any of the intracommunity transaction fields contain values, the system shall display a warning message:

*Warning Message:*
{quote}"For these transactions, in addition to the VAT return, you are required to submit the corresponding *VIES Statement* by the 25th day of the following month."
{quote}
h3. Warning Display Logic
 * Warning appears when any intracommunity field (Amount or Adjustment) contains non-zero values
 * Warning message displays the exact text specified above with "{*}VIES Statement{*}" in bold
 * Warning is classified as a warning (not error) allowing form submission to proceed
 * No impact on existing form functionality or performance

h3. Warning Persistence
 * Warning remains visible throughout form editing session
 * Warning disappears when all intracommunity fields are cleared/set to zero
 * Warning does not prevent form validation, saving, or submission

h3. User Experience
 * Warning appears in the standard warning notification area
 * Warning uses appropriate warning styling (amber/yellow color scheme)
 * Warning includes appropriate warning icon
 * Warning message is clearly readable and professionally formatted
